          <span>{tour.estimatedDuration ? `${tour.estimatedDuration} min` : "Duration not recorded"}</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Properties Viewed */}
      {propertiesLoading || ratingsLoading ? (
        <div className="animate-pulse mt-4 pt-4 border-t">
          <div className="h-4 bg-muted rounded w-1/4 mb-3"></div>
          <div className="h-16 bg-muted rounded"></div>
        </div>
      ) : propertiesError || ratingsError ? (
        <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-border">
          <p className="text-sm text-destructive">Failed to load property ratings</p>
        </div>
      ) : propertiesWithRatings.length > 0 ? (
        <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-border">
          <h4 className="font-medium text-sm mb-3">
            Properties Viewed ({propertiesWithRatings.length})
          </h4>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {propertiesWithRatings.map((property: any) => (
              <div 
                key={property.id}
                className="bg-muted/30 rounded-lg p-3 space-y-2"
                data-testid={`tour-property-${property.id}`}
              >
                <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                  <div className="flex-1">
                    <p className="font-medium text-sm">{property.address}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                      {property.bedrooms} bed • {property.bathrooms} bath • ${Number(property.price).toLocaleString()}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Rating Display or Rate Button */}
                {property.hasRating ? (
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    <div className="flex items-start gap-3 mt-2 p-2 bg-background rounded border">
                      <div className="flex-1">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                          <div className="flex">
                            {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((star) => (
                              <Star
                                key={star}
                                className={`h-3 w-3 ${
                                  star <= property.rating.rating
                                    ? "fill-yellow-400 text-yellow-400"
                                    : "text-gray-300"
                                }`}
                              />
                            ))}
                          </div>
                          <Badge 
                            variant="outline" 
                            className="text-xs"
                            data-testid={`rating-category-${property.id}`}
                          >
                            {property.rating.feedbackCategory === 'offer_now' && '🎯 Float Offer'}
                            {property.rating.feedbackCategory === 'hold_later' && '⏸️ Park for Future'}
                            {property.rating.feedbackCategory === 'reject' && '❌ Reject'}
                          </Badge>
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                          {property.rating.reason}
                        </p>
                        {property.rating.notes && (
                          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1 italic">
                            "{property.rating.notes}"
                          </p>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <Button
                      size="sm"
                      variant="outline"
                      className="w-full text-xs"
                      onClick={() => onViewMedia(property, tour.id, property.rating)}
                      data-testid={`button-view-media-${property.id}`}
                    >
                      <Camera className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                      View Photos & Documents
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    <Button
                      size="sm"
                      variant="outline"
                      className="w-full text-xs bg-primary/5 border-primary/20 text-primary hover:bg-primary/10"
                      onClick={() => onRateProperty(property.propertyId, tour.id, property.address)}
                      data-testid={`button-rate-property-${property.id}`}
                    >
                      <Star className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                      Rate This Property
                    </Button>
                    <Button
                      size="sm"
                      variant="outline"
                      className="w-full text-xs"
                      onClick={() => onViewMedia(property, tour.id, null)}
                      data-testid={`button-view-media-${property.id}`}
                    >
                      <Camera className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                      View Photos & Documents
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      ) : null}
    </div>
  );
}

export default function ClientDashboard() {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const { user, isAuthenticated, isLoading } = useAuth();
  const [showTourRequestModal, setShowTourRequestModal] = useState(false);
  const [selectedPropertyForPhotos, setSelectedPropertyForPhotos] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showClientTypeModal, setShowClientTypeModal] = useState(false);
  const [showRentalFormModal, setShowRentalFormModal] = useState(false);
  const [showRequirementsFormModal, setShowRequirementsFormModal] = useState(false);
  const [showOreaForm410Modal, setShowOreaForm410Modal] = useState(false);
  const [selectedPropertyForOrea, setSelectedPropertyForOrea] = useState<any>(null);
  const [showGroupDiscussionModal, setShowGroupDiscussionModal] = useState(false);
  const [selectedGroupId, setSelectedGroupId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showPropertyRatingModal, setShowPropertyRatingModal] = useState(false);
  const [selectedPropertyForRating, setSelectedPropertyForRating] = useState<{
    propertyId: string;
    tourId: string;
    address: string;
  } | null>(null);
  const [showPropertyMediaGallery, setShowPropertyMediaGallery] = useState(false);
  const [selectedPropertyForMedia, setSelectedPropertyForMedia] = useState<{
    property: any;
    tourId: string;
    rating: any;
  } | null>(null);
  const [showTourRemindersDialog, setShowTourRemindersDialog] = useState(false);
  const [selectedTourForReminders, setSelectedTourForReminders] = useState<{
    tourId: string;
    userId: string;
  } | null>(null);
  
  // Track if we've already shown the hard-gated modal to prevent re-opening
  const hasShownRequirementsModal = useRef(false);

  // Redirect to home if not authenticated
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isLoading && !isAuthenticated) {
      toast({
        title: "Unauthorized",
        description: "You are logged out. Logging in again...",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
      setTimeout(() => {
        window.location.href = "/api/login";
      }, 500);
      return;
    }
  }, [isAuthenticated, isLoading, toast]);

  // Fetch client requirements to check completion status
  const { data: clientRequirements, isLoading: requirementsLoading } = useQuery<{
    status: string;
    validationScore: string;
  } | null>({
    queryKey: ["/api/client-requirements"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated && user?.role === 'client',
    retry: false,
  });

  // Show client type selection modal for new clients
  useEffect(() => {
    if (user && user.role === 'client' && !user.clientType) {
      setShowClientTypeModal(true);
    }
  }, [user]);

  // Hard-gating: Show requirements modal ONLY if user has client type but NO requirements at all
  useEffect(() => {
    if (user && user.role === 'client' && user.clientType && !requirementsLoading && !hasShownRequirementsModal.current) {
      // Only show modal if requirements don't exist at all (not just incomplete)
      // Once user submits initial requirements, they can access dashboard even if incomplete
      const hasNoRequirements = !clientRequirements;
      
      if (hasNoRequirements && !showClientTypeModal) {
        if (user.clientType === 'buyer') {
          setShowRequirementsFormModal(true);
          hasShownRequirementsModal.current = true;
        } else if (user.clientType === 'renter') {
          setShowRentalFormModal(true);
          hasShownRequirementsModal.current = true;
        }
      }
    }
  }, [user, clientRequirements, requirementsLoading, showClientTypeModal]);

  // Fetch client statistics
  const { data: stats, isLoading: statsLoading } = useQuery<{
    propertiesSeen: number;
    propertiesRejected: number;
    offersMade: number;
    kmTraveled: number;
    timeInvested: number;
  }>({
    queryKey: ["/api/stats"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated,
  });

  // Fetch upcoming tours
  const { data: tours = [], isLoading: toursLoading } = useQuery<Tour[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/tours"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated,
  });

  // Fetch properties with tour data for recent viewing
  const { data: properties = [], isLoading: propertiesLoading } = useQuery<Property[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/properties"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated,
  });

  // Fetch offers
  const { data: offers = [], isLoading: offersLoading } = useQuery<Offer[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/offers"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated,
  });

  // Fetch agent information
  const { data: agent, isLoading: agentLoading } = useQuery<{
    id: string;
    firstName: string;
    lastName: string;
    email: string;
    profileImageUrl?: string;
  }>({
    queryKey: ["/api/auth/user/agent"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated,
    retry: false, // Don't retry on 404 errors
    throwOnError: false, // Don't throw errors for 404, handle gracefully
  });

  // Fetch client groups
  const { data: clientGroups = [], isLoading: groupsLoading } = useQuery<Array<{ id: string; name: string }>>({
    queryKey: ["/api/groups"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated,
  });

  const upcomingTours = tours.filter((tour: any) => {
    const tourDate = new Date(tour.scheduledDate);
    const now = new Date();
    return tourDate > now && tour.status !== "cancelled";
  });

  const pastTours = tours.filter((tour: any) => {
    const tourDate = new Date(tour.scheduledDate);
    const now = new Date();
    const isPast = tourDate <= now;
    
    // Show completed tours
    if (tour.status === "completed") return isPast;
    
    // Show legacy tours with no status (defensive for old data)
    if (!tour.status) return isPast;
    
    // Exclude all other statuses (cancelled, pending, scheduled, etc.)
    return false;
  }).sort((a: any, b: any) => new Date(b.scheduledDate).getTime() - new Date(a.scheduledDate).getTime());

  // Handle client type selection
  const handleClientTypeSelected = (clientType: "buyer" | "renter") => {
    setShowClientTypeModal(false);
    if (clientType === "renter") {
      setShowRentalFormModal(true);
    } else if (clientType === "buyer") {
      setShowRequirementsFormModal(true);
    }
    toast({
      title: "Welcome!",
      description: `You're set up as a ${clientType}. Let's complete your profile to find your perfect property.`,
    });
  };

  // Handle rental form completion
  const handleRentalFormComplete = () => {
    setShowRentalFormModal(false);
    toast({
      title: "Profile Complete",
      description: "Your rental preferences have been saved. We'll match you with suitable properties.",
    });
  };

  // Handle buyer requirements form completion
  const handleRequirementsFormComplete = () => {
    setShowRequirementsFormModal(false);
    toast({
      title: "Buyer Profile Complete",
      description: "Your buying requirements have been saved. We'll match you with suitable properties.",
    });
  };

  const getStatusColor = (status: string) => {
    switch (status) {
      case "viewed":
        return "bg-muted text-muted-foreground";
      case "liked":
        return "bg-green-100 text-green-700";
      case "rejected":
        return "bg-red-100 text-red-700";
      case "offer_made":
        return "bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700";
      default:
        return "bg-muted text-muted-foreground";
    }
  };

  if (!isAuthenticated || isLoading) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col bg-background">
      <Header userRole="client" />
      
      {/* Transparency Panel */}
      <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-primary/5 to-accent/5 border-b border-border">
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-6">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-4">Your Viewing Journey</h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-5 gap-4">
            <Card className="bg-card/80 backdrop-blur" data-testid="card-properties-seen">
              <CardContent className="p-4 text-center">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary" data-testid="text-properties-seen">
                  {statsLoading ? "..." : stats?.propertiesSeen || 0}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Properties Seen</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
            <Card className="bg-card/80 backdrop-blur" data-testid="card-properties-rejected">
              <CardContent className="p-4 text-center">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-destructive" data-testid="text-properties-rejected">
                  {statsLoading ? "..." : stats?.propertiesRejected || 0}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Rejected</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
            <Card className="bg-card/80 backdrop-blur" data-testid="card-offers-made">
              <CardContent className="p-4 text-center">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-yellow-600" data-testid="text-offers-made">
                  {statsLoading ? "..." : stats?.offersMade || 0}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Offers Made</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
            <Card className="bg-card/80 backdrop-blur" data-testid="card-km-traveled">
              <CardContent className="p-4 text-center">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-secondary" data-testid="text-km-traveled">
                  {statsLoading ? "..." : Math.round(stats?.kmTraveled || 0)}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">km Traveled</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
            <Card className="bg-card/80 backdrop-blur" data-testid="card-time-invested">
              <CardContent className="p-4 text-center">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-secondary" data-testid="text-time-invested">
                  {statsLoading ? "..." : stats?.timeInvested || 0}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Hours Invested</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <main className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
          
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-8">
            
            {/* Upcoming Tours & Recent Properties */}
            <div className="lg:col-span-2 space-y-6">
              
              {/* Upcoming Tours */}
              <Card>
                <div className="p-6 border-b border-border">
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                    <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">Upcoming Tours</h2>
                    <Button 
                      className="bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90"
                      onClick={() => setShowTourRequestModal(true)}
                      data-testid="button-request-tour"
                    >
                      <Plus className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                      Request Tour
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </div>
                
                <CardContent className="p-6">
                  {toursLoading ? (
                    <div className="animate-pulse border border-accent/20 bg-accent/5 rounded-lg p-4">
                      <div className="h-4 bg-muted rounded w-1/3 mb-2"></div>
                      <div className="h-3 bg-muted rounded w-1/2 mb-4"></div>
                      <div className="h-3 bg-muted rounded w-2/3"></div>
                    </div>
                  ) : upcomingTours.length === 0 ? (
                    <div className="text-center py-8">
                      <Calendar className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                      <p className="text-muted-foreground">No upcoming tours scheduled</p>
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <div className="space-y-4">
                      {upcomingTours.map((tour: any) => (
                        <div 
                          key={tour.id} 
                          className="border border-accent/20 bg-accent/5 rounded-lg p-4"
                          data-testid={`upcoming-tour-${tour.id}`}
                        >
                          <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
                            <div>
                              <div className="flex items-center space-x-2 mb-1">
                                <span className="font-medium">
                                  {tour.scheduledDate ? 
                                    new Date(tour.scheduledDate).toLocaleDateString() : 
                                    "Date TBD"
                                  }
                                </span>
                                <Badge className="bg-accent text-accent-foreground">
                                  {tour.status === "scheduled" ? "Confirmed" : tour.status}
                                </Badge>
                              </div>
                              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                                {tour.scheduledDate ? 
                                  new Date(tour.scheduledDate).toLocaleTimeString([], {
                                    hour: '2-digit',
                                    minute: '2-digit'
                                  }) : "Time TBD"
                                }
                              </p>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                          
                          <div className="space-y-2">
                            <div className="flex items-center text-sm">
                              <Home className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                              <span>Properties scheduled (details TBD)</span>
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex items-center text-sm">
                              <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                              <span>Areas to be determined</span>
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex items-center text-sm">
                              <Car className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                              <span>
                                {tour.totalDistance ? `~${tour.totalDistance} km total distance` : "Distance TBD"}
                              </span>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                          
                          <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-accent/20">
                            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                              <Button 
                                size="sm" 
                                className="bg-accent text-accent-foreground hover:bg-accent/90"
                                onClick={() => {
                                  setSelectedTourForReminders({
                                    tourId: tour.id,
                                    userId: user?.id || "",
                                  });
                                  setShowTourRemindersDialog(true);
                                }}
                                data-testid={`button-set-reminders-${tour.id}`}
                              >
                                <Bell className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" />
                                Set Reminders
                              </Button>
                              <Button 
                                size="sm" 
                                className="bg-accent text-accent-foreground hover:bg-accent/90"
                                data-testid="button-download-itinerary"
                              >
                                <Download className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" />
                                Download Itinerary
                              </Button>
                              <Button 
                                size="sm" 
                                variant="outline" 
                                className="border-accent text-accent hover:bg-accent/10"
                                data-testid="button-share-with-group"
                              >
                                <Share2 className="h-4 w-4 mr-1" />
                                Share with Group
                              </Button>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </CardContent>
              </Card>

              {/* Past Tours */}
              <Card>
                <div className="p-6 border-b border-border">
                  <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">Past Tours</h2>
                </div>
                
                <CardContent className="p-6">
                  {toursLoading ? (
                    <div className="animate-pulse border border-border rounded-lg p-4">
                      <div className="h-4 bg-muted rounded w-1/3 mb-2"></div>
                      <div className="h-3 bg-muted rounded w-1/2"></div>
                    </div>
                  ) : pastTours.length === 0 ? (
                    <div className="text-center py-8">
                      <History className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                      <p className="text-muted-foreground">No past tours yet</p>
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <div className="space-y-4">
                      {pastTours.slice(0, 5).map((tour: any) => (
                        <PastTourCard
                          key={tour.id}
                          tour={tour}
                          onRateProperty={(propertyId, tourId, address) => {
                            setSelectedPropertyForRating({ propertyId, tourId, address });
                            setShowPropertyRatingModal(true);
                          }}
                          onViewMedia={(property, tourId, rating) => {
                            setSelectedPropertyForMedia({ property, tourId, rating });
                            setShowPropertyMediaGallery(true);
                          }}
                        />
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </CardContent>
              </Card>

              {/* Recent Properties */}
              <Card>
                <div className="p-6 border-b border-border">
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold">Recent Properties</h3>
                </div>
                <CardContent className="p-6">
                  {propertiesLoading ? (
                    <div className="space-y-4">
                      {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => (
                        <div key={i} className="animate-pulse flex items-start space-x-4 p-4">
                          <div className="w-20 h-16 bg-muted rounded-md"></div>
                          <div className="flex-1">
                            <div className="h-4 bg-muted rounded w-1/3 mb-2"></div>
                            <div className="h-3 bg-muted rounded w-1/2 mb-1"></div>
                            <div className="h-3 bg-muted rounded w-2/3"></div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  ) : properties.length === 0 ? (
                    <div className="text-center py-8">
                      <Home className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                      <p className="text-muted-foreground">No properties viewed yet</p>
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <div className="space-y-4">
                      {properties.slice(0, 3).map((property: any) => (
                        <div 
                          key={property.id} 
                          className="flex items-start space-x-4 p-4 hover:bg-muted/50 rounded-lg transition-colors"
                          data-testid={`property-${property.id}`}
                        >
                          <PropertyPhoto
                            propertyId={property.id}
                            className="w-20 h-16"
                            showPhotoCount={true}
                            userRole={user?.role}
                          />
                          <div className="flex-1">
                            <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                              <div>
                                <h4 className="font-medium">{property.address}</h4>
                                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                                  {property.bedrooms} bed, {property.bathrooms} bath • ${Number(property.price).toLocaleString()}
                                </p>
                                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Recently added</p>
                              </div>
                              <Badge 
                                className={getStatusColor("viewed")}
                                data-testid={`status-viewed`}
                              >
                                Available
                              </Badge>
                            </div>
                            <div className="mt-2 flex space-x-2">
                              <Button 
                                size="sm" 
                                variant="ghost" 
                                className="text-xs h-6 px-2"
                                data-testid="button-view-photos"
                                onClick={() => setSelectedPropertyForPhotos(property.id)}
                              >
                                <Camera className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                                Photos
                              </Button>
                              <Button 
                                size="sm" 
                                variant="ghost" 
                                className="text-xs h-6 px-2 bg-primary/10 text-primary hover:bg-primary/20"
                                data-testid="button-request-viewing"
                              >
                                <Calendar className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                                Request Viewing
                              </Button>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </CardContent>
              </Card>
            </div>

            {/* Sidebar */}
            <div className="space-y-6">
              
              {/* Client Requirements Panel */}
              <ClientRequirementsPanel 
                onEdit={() => {
                  if (user?.clientType === 'buyer') {
                    setShowRequirementsFormModal(true);
                  } else if (user?.clientType === 'renter') {
                    setShowRentalFormModal(true);
                  }
                }}
              />
              
              {/* Group Collaboration */}
              <Card>
                <div className="p-6 border-b border-border">
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                    <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold">Your Group</h3>
                    <Button 
                      size="sm" 
                      variant="ghost" 
                      className="p-2"
                      data-testid="button-manage-group"
                    >
                      <Users className="h-4 w-4" />
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <CardContent className="p-6">
                  <div className="space-y-4">
                    <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
                      <Avatar className="h-8 w-8">
                        <AvatarFallback className="bg-primary text-primary-foreground">
                          {user?.firstName?.[0] || "U"}
                          {user?.lastName?.[0] || ""}
                        </AvatarFallback>
                      </Avatar>
                      <div>
                        <p className="font-medium text-sm">
                          {user?.firstName} {user?.lastName}
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">You</p>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  
                  <div className="mt-6 pt-4 border-t border-border">
                    <Button 
                      variant="ghost" 
                      className="w-full justify-start text-sm h-auto py-3"
                      data-testid="button-group-discussion"
                      onClick={() => {
                        if (clientGroups.length > 0) {
                          setSelectedGroupId(clientGroups[0].id);
                          setShowGroupDiscussionModal(true);
                        } else {
                          toast({
                            title: "No Group",
                            description: "You are not part of any group yet.",
                            variant: "destructive",
                          });
                        }
                      }}
                    >
                      <MessageCircle className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                      Group Discussion
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </CardContent>
              </Card>

              {/* Quick Actions */}
              <Card>
                <div className="p-6 border-b border-border">
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold">Quick Actions</h3>
                </div>
                <CardContent className="p-6 space-y-3">
                  <Button 
                    variant="ghost" 
                    className="w-full justify-start"
                    data-testid="button-view-shortlist"
                  >
                    <Heart className="h-4 w-4 mr-3" />
                    View Shortlist
                  </Button>
                  <Button 
                    variant="ghost" 
                    className="w-full justify-start"
                    data-testid="button-viewing-history"
                  >
                    <History className="h-4 w-4 mr-3" />
                    Viewing History
                  </Button>
                  
                  {user?.clientType === 'renter' && (
                    <Button 
                      variant="ghost" 
                      className="w-full justify-start bg-primary/5 text-primary hover:bg-primary/10"
                      onClick={() => {
                        // For now, use the first property. In production, user should select from available properties
                        const firstProperty = properties?.[0];
                        if (firstProperty) {
                          setSelectedPropertyForOrea(firstProperty);
                          setShowOreaForm410Modal(true);
                        } else {
                          toast({
                            title: "No Properties Available",
                            description: "Please contact your agent to add properties before submitting an application.",
                            variant: "destructive",
                          });
                        }
                      }}
                      data-testid="button-orea-form-410"
                    >
                      <Home className="h-4 w-4 mr-3" />
                      OREA Form 410 - Rental Application
                    </Button>
                  )}
                </CardContent>
              </Card>

              {/* Agent Contact */}
              <Card>
                <div className="p-6 border-b border-border">
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold">Your Agent</h3>
                </div>
                <CardContent className="p-6">
                  {agentLoading ? (
                    <div className="animate-pulse">
                      <div className="flex items-center space-x-3 mb-4">
                        <div className="h-12 w-12 bg-muted rounded-full"></div>
                        <div>
                          <div className="h-4 bg-muted rounded w-24 mb-2"></div>
                          <div className="h-3 bg-muted rounded w-32"></div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ) : agent ? (
                    <div className="flex items-center space-x-3 mb-4">
                      <Avatar className="h-12 w-12">
                        {agent.profileImageUrl ? (
                          <AvatarImage src={agent.profileImageUrl} alt={`${agent.firstName} ${agent.lastName}`} />
                        ) : (
                          <AvatarFallback className="bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground">
                            {agent.firstName?.[0]}{agent.lastName?.[0]}
                          </AvatarFallback>
                        )}
                      </Avatar>
                      <div>
                        <p className="font-medium">
                          {agent.firstName} {agent.lastName}
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                          {agent.email}
                        </p>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <div className="text-center py-4">
                      <p className="text-muted-foreground">No agent assigned</p>
                    </div>
                  )}
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    <Button 
                      className="w-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90"
                      data-testid="button-call-agent"
                    >
                      <Phone className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                      Call Agent
                    </Button>
                    <Button 
                      variant="outline" 
                      className="w-full"
                      data-testid="button-message-agent"
                    >
                      <MessageCircle className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                      Send Message
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </CardContent>
              </Card>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </main>

      <MobileNav userRole="client" />
      
      <TourRequestModal 
        isOpen={showTourRequestModal} 
        onClose={() => setShowTourRequestModal(false)} 
      />
      
      {selectedPropertyForPhotos && (
        <PhotoGalleryModal
          isOpen={!!selectedPropertyForPhotos}
          onClose={() => setSelectedPropertyForPhotos(null)}
          propertyId={selectedPropertyForPhotos}
          canUpload={user?.role === "agent"}
        />
      )}

      <ClientTypeSelectionModal 
        isOpen={showClientTypeModal}
        onClose={() => setShowClientTypeModal(false)}
        onClientTypeSelected={handleClientTypeSelected}
      />

      <RentalFormModal 
        isOpen={showRentalFormModal}
        onClose={() => setShowRentalFormModal(false)}
        onComplete={handleRentalFormComplete}
      />

      <RequirementsFormModal
        isOpen={showRequirementsFormModal}
        onClose={() => setShowRequirementsFormModal(false)}
        client={user}
      />

      <OreaForm410Modal 
        isOpen={showOreaForm410Modal}
        onClose={() => {
          setShowOreaForm410Modal(false);
          setSelectedPropertyForOrea(null);
        }}
        onComplete={() => {
          setShowOreaForm410Modal(false);
          setSelectedPropertyForOrea(null);
          toast({
            title: "Application Submitted",
            description: "Your OREA Form 410 rental application has been submitted successfully.",
          });
        }}
        selectedProperty={selectedPropertyForOrea}
      />

      {selectedGroupId && (
        <GroupDiscussionModal
          isOpen={showGroupDiscussionModal}
          onClose={() => {
            setShowGroupDiscussionModal(false);
            setSelectedGroupId(null);
          }}
          groupId={selectedGroupId}
        />
      )}

      {selectedPropertyForRating && (
        <PropertyRatingModal
          isOpen={showPropertyRatingModal}
          onClose={() => {
            setShowPropertyRatingModal(false);
            setSelectedPropertyForRating(null);
          }}
          propertyId={selectedPropertyForRating.propertyId}
          tourId={selectedPropertyForRating.tourId}
          propertyAddress={selectedPropertyForRating.address}
        />
      )}

      {selectedPropertyForMedia && (
        <PropertyMediaGallery
          open={showPropertyMediaGallery}
          onOpenChange={(open) => {
            setShowPropertyMediaGallery(open);
            if (!open) {
              setSelectedPropertyForMedia(null);
            }
          }}
          propertyId={selectedPropertyForMedia.property.propertyId}
          tourId={selectedPropertyForMedia.tourId}
          property={selectedPropertyForMedia.property}
          rating={selectedPropertyForMedia.rating}
        />
      )}

      {selectedTourForReminders && (
        <TourRemindersManager
          isOpen={showTourRemindersDialog}
          onClose={() => {
            setShowTourRemindersDialog(false);
            setSelectedTourForReminders(null);
          }}
          tourId={selectedTourForReminders.tourId}
          userId={selectedTourForReminders.userId}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

## FILE: client/src/pages/ClientsPage.tsx
```typescript
import { useState, useMemo } from "react";
import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useAuth } from "@/hooks/useAuth";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import type { User } from "@shared/schema";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Avatar, AvatarFallback, AvatarImage } from "@/components/ui/avatar";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select";
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
import { SidebarProvider, SidebarInset } from "@/components/ui/sidebar";
import TopAppBar from "@/components/TopAppBar";
import AgentSidebar from "@/components/AgentSidebar";
import MobileNav from "@/components/MobileNav";
import { 
  Search, 
  Users, 
  Plus, 
  Filter, 
  Home, 
  Building2, 
  Mail, 
  Phone,
  Calendar,
  MapPin,
  FileText,
  Heart,
  DollarSign,
  Star,
  MessageCircle,
  Settings
} from "lucide-react";
import ClientProfileModal from "@/components/ClientProfileModal";
import AddClientModal from "@/components/AddClientModal";

export default function ClientsPage() {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const { user, isAuthenticated } = useAuth();
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState("");
  const [clientTypeFilter, setClientTypeFilter] = useState<string>("all");
  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState<string>("all");
  const [selectedClient, setSelectedClient] = useState<any | null>(null);
  const [showClientProfile, setShowClientProfile] = useState(false);
  const [showAddClientModal, setShowAddClientModal] = useState(false);

  // Fetch clients for this agent
  const { data: clients = [], isLoading } = useQuery<any[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated && user?.role === "agent",
  });

  // Filter and search clients
  const filteredClients = useMemo(() => {
    return clients.filter(client => {
      const matchesSearch = !searchQuery || 
        `${client.firstName} ${client.lastName}`.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
        client.email?.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
      
      const matchesType = clientTypeFilter === "all" || client.clientType === clientTypeFilter;
      
      const matchesStatus = statusFilter === "all" || 
        (statusFilter === "active" && client.stats?.lastActivity) ||
        (statusFilter === "new" && !client.stats?.totalTours);
      
      return matchesSearch && matchesType && matchesStatus;
    });
  }, [clients, searchQuery, clientTypeFilter, statusFilter]);

  const handleClientClick = (client: ClientWithProfile) => {
    setSelectedClient(client);
    setShowClientProfile(true);
  };

  const getClientStatusBadge = (client: ClientWithProfile) => {
    if (!client.stats?.totalTours) {
      return <Badge variant="secondary" data-testid={`badge-new-${client.id}`}>New</Badge>;
    }
    if (client.stats?.activeOffers > 0) {
      return <Badge variant="destructive" data-testid={`badge-active-offers-${client.id}`}>Active Offers</Badge>;
    }
    if (client.stats?.lastActivity) {
      const daysSinceActivity = Math.floor((Date.now() - new Date(client.stats.lastActivity).getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
      if (daysSinceActivity <= 7) {
        return <Badge variant="default" data-testid={`badge-active-${client.id}`}>Active</Badge>;
      }
    }
    return <Badge variant="outline" data-testid={`badge-inactive-${client.id}`}>Inactive</Badge>;
  };

  if (!isAuthenticated || user?.role !== "agent") {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen">
        <Card>
          <CardContent className="p-6">
            <p className="text-muted-foreground">Access denied. This page is for agents only.</p>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <SidebarProvider>
      <div className="min-h-screen flex w-full bg-background">
        <AgentSidebar 
          activeSection="clients"
          onSectionChange={() => {}}
          pendingRequests={0}
          upcomingTours={0}
        />
        
        <SidebarInset className="flex-1 flex flex-col">
          <TopAppBar 
            userRole="agent"
            onCreateTour={() => {}}
            onApproveRequests={() => {}}
            onRequestDocs={() => {}}
            onStartIntake={() => {}}
            onShowBranding={() => {}}
            onShowIntegrations={() => {}}
            onShowNotifications={() => {}}
          />
          
          <main className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
            <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
              {/* Header */}
              <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center justify-between mb-6">
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-2" data-testid="title-clients">Clients</h1>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground">
              Manage your client relationships and track their property journey
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-4 md:mt-0">
            <Button 
              variant="outline" 
              size="sm"
              data-testid="button-import-clients"
            >
              <Users className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
              Import Clients
            </Button>
            <Button 
              size="sm"
              onClick={() => setShowAddClientModal(true)}
              data-testid="button-add-client"
            >
              <Plus className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
              Add Client
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Statistics Cards */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-6">
          <Card data-testid="card-total-clients">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <Users className="h-8 w-8 text-primary bg-primary/10 rounded p-1" />
                <div className="ml-3">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground">Total Clients</p>
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold" data-testid="text-total-clients">{clients.length}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
          
          <Card data-testid="card-buyers">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <Home className="h-8 w-8 text-blue-600 bg-blue-100 rounded p-1" />
                <div className="ml-3">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground">Buyers</p>
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold" data-testid="text-buyers">
                    {clients.filter(c => c.clientType === "buyer").length}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
          
          <Card data-testid="card-renters">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <Building2 className="h-8 w-8 text-green-600 bg-green-100 rounded p-1" />
                <div className="ml-3">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground">Renters</p>
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold" data-testid="text-renters">
                    {clients.filter(c => c.clientType === "renter").length}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
          
          <Card data-testid="card-active-offers">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <DollarSign className="h-8 w-8 text-orange-600 bg-orange-100 rounded p-1" />
                <div className="ml-3">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground">Active Offers</p>
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold" data-testid="text-active-offers">
                    {clients.reduce((sum, c) => sum + (c.stats?.activeOffers || 0), 0)}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        </div>

        {/* Filters and Search */}
        <Card className="mb-6">
          <CardContent className="p-4">
            <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-4">
              <div className="flex-1">
                <div className="relative">
                  <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground h-4 w-4" />
                  <Input
                    placeholder="Search clients by name or email..."
                    value={searchQuery}
                    onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                    className="pl-9"
                    data-testid="input-search-clients"
                  />
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <Select value={clientTypeFilter} onValueChange={setClientTypeFilter}>
                <SelectTrigger className="w-full md:w-[180px]" data-testid="select-client-type">
                  <SelectValue placeholder="Client Type" />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  <SelectItem value="all">All Types</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="buyer">Buyers</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="renter">Renters</SelectItem>
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
              
              <Select value={statusFilter} onValueChange={setStatusFilter}>
                <SelectTrigger className="w-full md:w-[180px]" data-testid="select-status">
                  <SelectValue placeholder="Status" />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  <SelectItem value="all">All Status</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="active">Active</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="new">New</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="inactive">Inactive</SelectItem>
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
              
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" data-testid="button-advanced-filters">
                <Filter className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                More Filters
              </Button>
            </div>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* Clients List */}
        <Card>
          <CardHeader>
            <CardTitle className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <span>Client List ({filteredClients.length})</span>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                <span>Sorted by Recent Activity</span>
              </div>
            </CardTitle>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent>
            {isLoading ? (
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => (
                  <div key={i} className="flex items-center space-x-4 p-4 border rounded-lg animate-pulse">
                    <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-muted rounded-full"></div>
                    <div className="flex-1 space-y-2">
                      <div className="h-4 bg-muted rounded w-1/4"></div>
                      <div className="h-3 bg-muted rounded w-1/2"></div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            ) : filteredClients.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="text-center py-12">
                <Users className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No clients found</h3>
                <p className="text-muted-foreground mb-4">
                  {searchQuery || clientTypeFilter !== "all" || statusFilter !== "all" 
                    ? "Try adjusting your filters" 
                    : "Start by adding your first client"}
                </p>
                <Button 
                  onClick={() => setShowAddClientModal(true)}
                  data-testid="button-add-first-client"
                >
                  <Plus className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Add Your First Client
                </Button>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {filteredClients.map((client) => (
                  <div 
                    key={client.id}
                    className="flex items-center space-x-4 p-4 border rounded-lg hover:bg-muted/50 cursor-pointer transition-colors"
                    onClick={() => handleClientClick(client)}
                    data-testid={`client-row-${client.id}`}
                  >
                    <Avatar className="h-12 w-12">
                      <AvatarImage 
                        src={client.profileImageUrl || ""} 
                        alt={`${client.firstName} ${client.lastName}`} 
                      />
                      <AvatarFallback>
                        {client.firstName?.[0]}{client.lastName?.[0]}
                      </AvatarFallback>
                    </Avatar>
                    
                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                        <h3 className="font-semibold text-lg" data-testid={`text-client-name-${client.id}`}>
                          {client.firstName} {client.lastName}
                        </h3>
                        {getClientStatusBadge(client)}
                        {client.clientType && (
                          <Badge variant="outline" data-testid={`badge-type-${client.id}`}>
                            {client.clientType === "buyer" ? "Buyer" : "Renter"}
                          </Badge>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                        <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                          <Mail className="h-3 w-3" />
                          {client.email}
                        </span>
                        {client.rentalProfile && (
                          <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                            <DollarSign className="h-3 w-3" />
                            ${Number(client.rentalProfile.monthlyBudget).toLocaleString()}/mo
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3 text-sm">
                      <div className="text-center">
                        <p className="font-semibold" data-testid={`text-tours-${client.id}`}>
                          {client.stats?.totalTours || 0}
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Tours</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-center">
                        <p className="font-semibold" data-testid={`text-shortlisted-${client.id}`}>
                          {client.stats?.shortlistedProperties || 0}
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Shortlisted</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-center">
                        <p className="font-semibold" data-testid={`text-offers-${client.id}`}>
                          {client.stats?.activeOffers || 0}
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Offers</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-center">
                        <p className="font-semibold text-red-600" data-testid={`text-rejected-${client.id}`}>
                          {client.stats?.propertiesRejected || 0}
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Rejected</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-center">
                        <p className="font-semibold text-blue-600" data-testid={`text-km-travelled-${client.id}`}>
                          {client.stats?.kmTravelled || 0}
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">km Travelled</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-center">
                        <p className="font-semibold text-purple-600" data-testid={`text-hours-invested-${client.id}`}>
                          {client.stats?.hoursInvested || 0}
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Hours Invested</p>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      <Button 
                        variant="ghost" 
                        size="sm"
                        onClick={(e) => {
                          e.stopPropagation();
                          toast({
                            title: "Feature Coming Soon",
                            description: "Direct messaging will be available soon.",
                          });
                        }}
                        data-testid={`button-message-${client.id}`}
                      >
                        <MessageCircle className="h-4 w-4" />
                      </Button>
                      <Button 
                        variant="ghost" 
                        size="sm"
                        onClick={(e) => {
                          e.stopPropagation();
                          handleClientClick(client);
                        }}
                        data-testid={`button-view-profile-${client.id}`}
                      >
                        <Settings className="h-4 w-4" />
                      </Button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* Client Profile Modal */}
        {selectedClient && (
          <ClientProfileModal
            isOpen={showClientProfile}
            onClose={() => {
              setShowClientProfile(false);
              setSelectedClient(null);
            }}
            client={selectedClient}
          />
        )}

        {/* Add Client Modal */}
        <AddClientModal
          isOpen={showAddClientModal}
          onClose={() => setShowAddClientModal(false)}
        />
              </div>
            </main>
          </SidebarInset>
        </div>
        <MobileNav userRole="agent" />
      </SidebarProvider>
    );
  }```

## FILE: client/src/pages/DocumentsPage.tsx
```typescript
import { useState } from "react";
import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useAuth } from "@/hooks/useAuth";
import Header from "@/components/Header";
import AgentSidebar from "@/components/AgentSidebar";
import { SidebarProvider, SidebarInset } from "@/components/ui/sidebar";
import DocumentCenterModal from "@/components/DocumentCenterModal";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { FileText, Upload, Download, Folder, Plus } from "lucide-react";

export default function DocumentsPage() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [showDocumentCenter, setShowDocumentCenter] = useState(false);

  // Fetch documents for the agent
  const { data: documents = [], isLoading } = useQuery<any[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/documents"],
    enabled: !!user && user.role === 'agent',
  });

  const getDocumentTypeColor = (type: string) => {
    switch (type) {
      case 'offer_placed': return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
      case 'offer_received': return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800';
      case 'representative_agreement': return 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-800';
      case 'rental_application': return 'bg-orange-100 text-orange-800';
      case 'client_id': return 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800';
      default: return 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800';
    }
  };

  if (!user) {
    return <div>Loading...</div>;
  }

  return (
    <SidebarProvider>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
        <Header userRole={user.role} />
        <div className="flex">
          <AgentSidebar />
          <SidebarInset>
            <main className="flex-1 p-6">
          <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">Documents</h1>
              <p className="text-muted-foreground">Manage client documents and forms</p>
            </div>
            <Button 
              onClick={() => setShowDocumentCenter(true)}
              className="gap-2"
              data-testid="button-upload-document"
            >
              <Upload className="h-4 w-4" />
              Upload Document
            </Button>
          </div>

          {isLoading ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
              <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-8 w-8 border-b-2 border-primary"></div>
            </div>
          ) : documents.length === 0 ? (
            <Card>
              <CardContent className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-12">
                <FileText className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mb-4" />
                <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No documents uploaded</h3>
                <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center mb-4">
                  Upload client documents, forms, and agreements to get started.
                </p>
                <Button 
                  onClick={() => setShowDocumentCenter(true)}
                  className="gap-2"
                >
                  <Upload className="h-4 w-4" />
                  Upload First Document
                </Button>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
          ) : (
            <div className="grid gap-4">
              {documents.map((doc) => (
                <Card key={doc.id} className="hover:shadow-md transition-shadow">
                  <CardContent className="p-4">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                        <FileText className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground" />
                        <div>
                          <h3 className="font-medium">{doc.title || doc.fileName}</h3>
                          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                            Uploaded by {doc.uploadedBy}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <Badge className={getDocumentTypeColor(doc.documentType)}>
                          {doc.documentType.replace('_', ' ')}
                        </Badge>
                        <Button variant="outline" size="sm">
                          <Download className="h-4 w-4" />
                        </Button>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </CardContent>
                </Card>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}

            </main>
          </SidebarInset>
        </div>
      </div>

      <DocumentCenterModal
        isOpen={showDocumentCenter}
        onClose={() => setShowDocumentCenter(false)}
        userId={user.id}
      />
    </SidebarProvider>
  );
}```

## FILE: client/src/pages/MediaPage.tsx
```typescript
import { useState } from "react";
import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useAuth } from "@/hooks/useAuth";
import Header from "@/components/Header";
import AgentSidebar from "@/components/AgentSidebar";
import { SidebarProvider, SidebarInset } from "@/components/ui/sidebar";
import PhotoUploadModal from "@/components/PhotoUploadModal";
import PhotoGalleryModal from "@/components/PhotoGalleryModal";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Camera, Upload, Image, Video, Play } from "lucide-react";
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { RadioGroup, RadioGroupItem } from "@/components/ui/radio-group";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import type { Property } from "@shared/schema";

export default function MediaPage() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [showPhotoUpload, setShowPhotoUpload] = useState(false);
  const [showPhotoGallery, setShowPhotoGallery] = useState(false);
  const [showPropertySelector, setShowPropertySelector] = useState(false);
  const [selectedProperty, setSelectedProperty] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [uploadPropertyId, setUploadPropertyId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [tempSelectedPropertyId, setTempSelectedPropertyId] = useState<string>("");

  // Fetch properties
  const { data: properties = [] } = useQuery<Property[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/properties"],
    enabled: !!user && user.role === 'agent',
  });

  // Fetch media/photos for properties
  const { data: photos = [], isLoading } = useQuery<any[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/photos"],
    enabled: !!user && user.role === 'agent',
  });

  const handleUploadClick = () => {
    if (properties.length === 0) {
      return;
    }
    if (properties.length === 1) {
      setUploadPropertyId(properties[0].id);
      setShowPhotoUpload(true);
    } else {
      setTempSelectedPropertyId(properties[0].id);
      setShowPropertySelector(true);
    }
  };

  const handlePropertySelected = () => {
    if (tempSelectedPropertyId) {
      setUploadPropertyId(tempSelectedPropertyId);
      setShowPropertySelector(false);
      setShowPhotoUpload(true);
    }
  };

  const handleViewGallery = (propertyId: string) => {
    setSelectedProperty(propertyId);
    setShowPhotoGallery(true);
  };

  if (!user) {
    return <div>Loading...</div>;
  }

  return (
    <SidebarProvider>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
        <Header userRole={user.role} />
        <div className="flex">
          <AgentSidebar />
          <SidebarInset>
            <main className="flex-1 p-6">
          <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">Media</h1>
              <p className="text-muted-foreground">Manage property photos and videos</p>
            </div>
            <Button 
              onClick={handleUploadClick}
              className="gap-2"
              data-testid="button-upload-photo"
              disabled={properties.length === 0}
            >
              <Upload className="h-4 w-4" />
              Upload Media
            </Button>
          </div>

          {isLoading ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
              <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-8 w-8 border-b-2 border-primary"></div>
            </div>
          ) : photos.length === 0 ? (
            <Card>
              <CardContent className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-12">
                <Camera className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mb-4" />
                <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No media uploaded</h3>
                <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center mb-4">
                  Upload property photos and videos to showcase your listings.
                </p>
                <Button 
                  onClick={handleUploadClick}
                  className="gap-2"
                  disabled={properties.length === 0}
                >
                  <Camera className="h-4 w-4" />
                  Upload First Photo
                </Button>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
          ) : (
            <div className="grid gap-6">
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 lg:grid-cols-6 gap-4">
                {photos.map((photo) => (
                  <Card key={photo.id} className="overflow-hidden hover:shadow-md transition-shadow cursor-pointer"
                        onClick={() => handleViewGallery(photo.propertyId)}>
                    <div className="aspect-square relative">
                      <img 
                        src={photo.url} 
                        alt={photo.caption || 'Property photo'}
                        className="w-full h-full object-cover"
                      />
                      <div className="absolute top-2 right-2">
                        <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-xs">
                          <Image className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                          Photo
                        </Badge>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <CardContent className="p-2">
                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
                        {photo.caption || 'Untitled'}
                      </p>
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

            </main>
          </SidebarInset>
        </div>
      </div>

      <Dialog open={showPropertySelector} onOpenChange={setShowPropertySelector}>
        <DialogContent data-testid="dialog-property-selector">
          <DialogHeader>
            <DialogTitle>Select Property</DialogTitle>
          </DialogHeader>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Choose which property to upload media for:</p>
            <RadioGroup value={tempSelectedPropertyId} onValueChange={setTempSelectedPropertyId}>
              {properties.map((property) => (
                <div key={property.id} className="flex items-center space-x-2 p-2 hover:bg-muted rounded">
                  <RadioGroupItem value={property.id} id={property.id} />
                  <Label htmlFor={property.id} className="flex-1 cursor-pointer">
                    <div className="font-medium">{property.address}</div>
                    <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                      {property.propertyType} · ${property.price?.toLocaleString()}
                    </div>
                  </Label>
                </div>
              ))}
            </RadioGroup>
            <div className="flex justify-end gap-2">
              <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowPropertySelector(false)}>Cancel</Button>
              <Button onClick={handlePropertySelected} disabled={!tempSelectedPropertyId}>Continue</Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </DialogContent>
      </Dialog>

      {uploadPropertyId && (
        <PhotoUploadModal
          isOpen={showPhotoUpload}
          onClose={() => {
            setShowPhotoUpload(false);
            setUploadPropertyId(null);
          }}
          propertyId={uploadPropertyId}
        />
      )}

      {selectedProperty && (
        <PhotoGalleryModal
          isOpen={showPhotoGallery}
          onClose={() => {
            setShowPhotoGallery(false);
            setSelectedProperty(null);
          }}
          propertyId={selectedProperty}
        />
      )}
    </SidebarProvider>
  );
}```

import { useState } from "react";

export default function ReportsPage() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [showTourReport, setShowTourReport] = useState(false);
  const [showClientHistory, setShowClientHistory] = useState(false);
  const [showProductivityDashboard, setShowProductivityDashboard] = useState(false);
  const [selectedClientId, setSelectedClientId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Fetch clients for client history selection
  const { data: clients = [] } = useQuery<any[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients"],
    enabled: !!user && user.role === 'agent',
  });

  // Fetch reports data
  const { data: stats, isLoading } = useQuery<{
    todayTours?: number;
    activeClients?: number;
    pendingRequests?: number;
    weeklyDistance?: number;
  }>({
    queryKey: ["/api/stats"],
    enabled: !!user && user.role === 'agent',
  });

  const reportTypes = [
    {
      title: "Tour Report",
      description: "Post-tour performance and client feedback",
      icon: Calendar,
      action: "Generate",
      available: true
    },
