      title: "Client History Ledger",
      description: "Complete client interaction timeline",
      icon: Users,
      action: "Export",
      available: true
    },
    {
      title: "Productivity Dashboard",
      description: "Agent performance metrics and KPIs",
      icon: TrendingUp,
      action: "View",
      available: true
    },
    {
      title: "Scope Fit Over Time",
      description: "Property matching accuracy trends",
      icon: BarChart,
      action: "Analyze",
      available: false
    },
    {
      title: "Location Analytics",
      description: "Geographic tour patterns and efficiency",
      icon: MapPin,
      action: "Generate",
      available: false
    }
  ];

  if (!user) {
    return <div>Loading...</div>;
  }

  return (
    <SidebarProvider>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
        <Header userRole={user.role} />
        <div className="flex">
          <AgentSidebar />
          <SidebarInset>
            <main className="flex-1 p-6">
          <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">Reports</h1>
              <p className="text-muted-foreground">Generate insights and export data</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Quick Stats */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-4 gap-6 mb-8">
            <Card>
              <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
                <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Today's Tours</CardTitle>
                <Calendar className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
              </CardHeader>
              <CardContent>
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats?.todayTours || 0}</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
            
            <Card>
              <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
                <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Active Clients</CardTitle>
                <Users className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
              </CardHeader>
              <CardContent>
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats?.activeClients || 0}</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>

            <Card>
              <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
                <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Pending Requests</CardTitle>
                <Badge className="h-4 w-4" />
              </CardHeader>
              <CardContent>
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats?.pendingRequests || 0}</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>

            <Card>
              <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-2">
                <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Weekly Distance</CardTitle>
                <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
              </CardHeader>
              <CardContent>
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{stats?.weeklyDistance || 0} km</div>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
          </div>

          {/* Report Types */}
          <div className="grid gap-6">
            <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">Available Reports</h2>
            <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
              {reportTypes.map((report) => {
                // Special rendering for Client History Ledger
                if (report.title === "Client History Ledger") {
                  return (
                    <Card key={report.title} className="hover:shadow-md transition-shadow">
                      <CardHeader>
                        <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-3">
                          <report.icon className="h-5 w-5" />
                          {report.title}
                        </CardTitle>
                      </CardHeader>
                      <CardContent className="space-y-4">
                        <p className="text-muted-foreground">{report.description}</p>
                        <div className="space-y-2">
                          <label className="text-sm font-medium">Select Client</label>
                          <Select
                            value={selectedClientId || ""}
                            onValueChange={setSelectedClientId}
                            data-testid="select-client-for-history"
                          >
                            <SelectTrigger>
                              <SelectValue placeholder="Choose a client" />
                            </SelectTrigger>
                            <SelectContent>
                              {clients.map((client: any) => (
                                <SelectItem key={client.id} value={client.id}>
                                  {client.firstName} {client.lastName}
                                </SelectItem>
                              ))}
                            </SelectContent>
                          </Select>
                        </div>
                        <Button 
                          disabled={!selectedClientId}
                          onClick={() => setShowClientHistory(true)}
                          className="w-full gap-2"
                          data-testid="button-client-history-ledger"
                        >
                          <Download className="h-4 w-4" />
                          {report.action} Report
                        </Button>
                      </CardContent>
                    </Card>
                  );
                }
                
                // Standard rendering for other reports
                return (
                  <Card key={report.title} className="hover:shadow-md transition-shadow">
                    <CardHeader>
                      <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-3">
                        <report.icon className="h-5 w-5" />
                        {report.title}
                      </CardTitle>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent>
                      <p className="text-muted-foreground mb-4">{report.description}</p>
                      <Button 
                        disabled={!report.available}
                        onClick={() => {
                          if (report.title === "Tour Report") {
                            setShowTourReport(true);
                          } else if (report.title === "Productivity Dashboard") {
                            setShowProductivityDashboard(true);
                          }
                        }}
                        className="w-full gap-2"
                        data-testid={`button-${report.title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`}
                      >
                        <Download className="h-4 w-4" />
                        {report.action} Report
                      </Button>
                      {!report.available && (
                        <Badge variant="secondary" className="mt-2">
                          Coming Soon
                        </Badge>
                      )}
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Modals */}
          <TourReportModal 
            isOpen={showTourReport} 
            onClose={() => setShowTourReport(false)} 
          />
          <ClientHistoryModal
            isOpen={showClientHistory}
            onClose={() => setShowClientHistory(false)}
            selectedClientId={selectedClientId}
          />
          <ProductivityDashboardModal
            isOpen={showProductivityDashboard}
            onClose={() => setShowProductivityDashboard(false)}
          />
            </main>
          </SidebarInset>
        </div>
      </div>
    </SidebarProvider>
  );
}```

## FILE: client/src/pages/RequirementsHub.tsx
```typescript
import { useState } from "react";
import { useQuery, useMutation } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useAuth } from "@/hooks/useAuth";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { apiRequest, queryClient } from "@/lib/queryClient";
import Header from "@/components/Header";
import MobileNav from "@/components/MobileNav";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle, CardDescription } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area";
import { Avatar, AvatarFallback, AvatarImage } from "@/components/ui/avatar";
import { Progress } from "@/components/ui/progress";
import {
  Select,
  SelectContent,
  SelectItem,
  SelectTrigger,
  SelectValue,
} from "@/components/ui/select";
import {
  Table,
  TableBody,
  TableCell,
  TableHead,
  TableHeader,
  TableRow,
} from "@/components/ui/table";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogFooter,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
import {
  Target,
  TrendingUp,
  Shield,
  Clock,
  CheckCircle,
  XCircle,
  AlertTriangle,
  FileText,
  History,
  Home,
  DollarSign,
  MapPin,
  Users,
  Plus,
  Eye,
  Check,
  X,
  Calendar,
  Sparkles,
} from "lucide-react";
import { format } from "date-fns";

export default function RequirementsHub() {
  const { user, isAuthenticated, isLoading: authLoading } = useAuth();
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const [selectedClientId, setSelectedClientId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showExceptionModal, setShowExceptionModal] = useState(false);
  const [exceptionType, setExceptionType] = useState<string>("");
  const [exceptionDescription, setExceptionDescription] = useState("");
  const [exceptionJustification, setExceptionJustification] = useState("");

  // Fetch all clients for agent
  const { data: clients = [], isLoading: clientsLoading } = useQuery<any[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients"],
    enabled: isAuthenticated && user?.role === "agent",
  });

  // Fetch enhanced requirements data for selected client
  const { data: requirementsData, isLoading: requirementsLoading } = useQuery<any>({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", selectedClientId, "requirements-enhanced"],
    enabled: !!selectedClientId,
  });

  // Create exception mutation
  const createExceptionMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (data: any) => {
      const response = await apiRequest(
        "POST",
        `/api/requirements/${requirementsData?.requirement?.id}/exceptions`,
        data
      );
      return response.json();
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["/api/clients", selectedClientId, "requirements-enhanced"] });
      toast({
        title: "Exception Created",
        description: "The requirement exception has been added successfully.",
      });
      setShowExceptionModal(false);
      setExceptionType("");
      setExceptionDescription("");
      setExceptionJustification("");
    },
    onError: (error: any) => {
      toast({
        title: "Error",
        description: error.message || "Failed to create exception.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    },
  });

  // Validate requirements mutation
  const validateRequirementsMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async () => {
      const response = await apiRequest(
        "POST",
        `/api/requirements/${requirementsData?.requirement?.id}/validate`,
        {}
      );
      return response.json();
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["/api/clients", selectedClientId, "requirements-enhanced"] });
      toast({
        title: "Requirements Validated",
        description: "Client requirements have been validated successfully.",
      });
    },
    onError: (error: any) => {
      toast({
        title: "Error",
        description: error.message || "Failed to validate requirements.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    },
  });

  const handleCreateException = () => {
    if (!exceptionType || !exceptionDescription || !exceptionJustification) {
      toast({
        title: "Missing Fields",
        description: "Please fill in all exception fields.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
      return;
    }

    createExceptionMutation.mutate({
      exceptionType,
      description: exceptionDescription,
      justification: exceptionJustification,
    });
  };

  const requirement = requirementsData?.requirement;
  const versions = requirementsData?.versions || [];
  const exceptions = requirementsData?.exceptions || [];
  const propertyMatches = requirementsData?.propertyMatches || [];

  const getValidationScoreColor = (score: number) => {
    if (score >= 0.8) return "text-green-600";
    if (score >= 0.5) return "text-yellow-600";
    return "text-red-600";
  };

  const getValidationScoreLabel = (score: number) => {
    if (score >= 0.8) return "Complete";
    if (score >= 0.5) return "Partial";
    return "Incomplete";
  };

  const getMatchScoreColor = (score: number) => {
    if (score >= 0.7) return "bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900 dark:text-green-200";
    if (score >= 0.5) return "bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 dark:bg-yellow-900 dark:text-yellow-200";
    return "bg-red-100 text-red-800 dark:bg-red-900 dark:text-red-200";
  };

  if (authLoading || !isAuthenticated) {
    return <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen">Loading...</div>;
  }

  if (user?.role !== "agent") {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen">
        <p>Access denied. This page is only available to agents.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-900">
      <Header userRole={user?.role || "client"} />
      <div className="container mx-auto p-4 md:p-6 space-y-6 pb-20 md:pb-6">
        {/* Page Header */}
        <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center md:justify-between gap-4">
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold flex items-center gap-2" data-testid="text-page-title">
              <Target className="h-8 w-8" />
              Requirements Hub
            </h1>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground mt-1">
              Manage client requirements, scope fit scoring, and exceptions
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Client Selection */}
        <Card>
          <CardHeader>
            <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <Users className="h-5 w-5" />
              Select Client
            </CardTitle>
            <CardDescription>
              Choose a client to view their requirements and property matches
            </CardDescription>
          </CardHeader>
          <CardContent>
            <Select value={selectedClientId || ""} onValueChange={setSelectedClientId}>
              <SelectTrigger data-testid="select-client">
                <SelectValue placeholder="Select a client" />
              </SelectTrigger>
              <SelectContent>
                {clients.map((client: any) => (
                  <SelectItem key={client.id} value={client.id}>
                    {client.firstName} {client.lastName} - {client.clientType || "buyer"}
                  </SelectItem>
                ))}
              </SelectContent>
            </Select>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* Requirements Data Display */}
        {selectedClientId && (
          <>
            {requirementsLoading ? (
              <Card>
                <CardContent className="py-8">
                  <p className="text-center text-muted-foreground">Loading requirements...</p>
                </CardContent>
              </Card>
            ) : !requirement ? (
              <Card>
                <CardContent className="py-8">
                  <p className="text-center text-muted-foreground">
                    No requirements found for this client. They need to complete their profile.
                  </p>
                </CardContent>
              </Card>
            ) : (
              <Tabs defaultValue="overview" className="space-y-4">
                <TabsList className="grid w-full grid-cols-4 lg:w-auto">
                  <TabsTrigger value="overview" data-testid="tab-overview">
                    <Target className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                    Overview
                  </TabsTrigger>
                  <TabsTrigger value="matches" data-testid="tab-matches">
                    <Sparkles className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                    Matches
                  </TabsTrigger>
                  <TabsTrigger value="exceptions" data-testid="tab-exceptions">
                    <Shield className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                    Exceptions
                  </TabsTrigger>
                  <TabsTrigger value="history" data-testid="tab-history">
                    <History className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                    History
                  </TabsTrigger>
                </TabsList>

                {/* Overview Tab */}
                <TabsContent value="overview" className="space-y-4">
                  <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4">
                    {/* Validation Score Card */}
                    <Card>
                      <CardHeader className="pb-3">
                        <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Validation Score</CardTitle>
                      </CardHeader>
                      <CardContent>
                        <div className="text-2xl font-bold" data-testid="text-validation-score">
                          {(parseFloat(requirement.validationScore) * 100).toFixed(0)}%
                        </div>
                        <Progress
                          value={parseFloat(requirement.validationScore) * 100}
                          className="mt-2"
                        />
                        <p className={`text-sm mt-2 ${getValidationScoreColor(parseFloat(requirement.validationScore))}`}>
                          {getValidationScoreLabel(parseFloat(requirement.validationScore))}
                        </p>
                      </CardContent>
                    </Card>

                    {/* Status Card */}
                    <Card>
                      <CardHeader className="pb-3">
                        <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Status</CardTitle>
                      </CardHeader>
                      <CardContent>
                        <Badge className="text-sm" data-testid="badge-status">
                          {requirement.status}
                        </Badge>
                        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-2">
                          Version {requirement.version}
                        </p>
                      </CardContent>
                    </Card>

                    {/* Property Matches Card */}
                    <Card>
                      <CardHeader className="pb-3">
                        <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Property Matches</CardTitle>
                      </CardHeader>
                      <CardContent>
                        <div className="text-2xl font-bold" data-testid="text-match-count">
                          {propertyMatches.length}
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-2">
                          Properties in scope
                        </p>
                      </CardContent>
                    </Card>

                    {/* Exceptions Card */}
                    <Card>
                      <CardHeader className="pb-3">
                        <CardTitle className="text-sm font-medium">Exceptions</CardTitle>
                      </CardHeader>
                      <CardContent>
                        <div className="text-2xl font-bold" data-testid="text-exception-count">
                          {exceptions.length}
                        </div>
                        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-2">
                          Active exceptions
                        </p>
                      </CardContent>
                    </Card>
                  </div>

                  {/* Requirements Details */}
                  <Card>
                    <CardHeader>
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                        <CardTitle>Requirements Details</CardTitle>
                        <Button
                          onClick={() => validateRequirementsMutation.mutate()}
                          disabled={validateRequirementsMutation.isPending}
                          data-testid="button-validate"
                        >
                          <CheckCircle className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                          Validate
                        </Button>
                      </div>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent className="space-y-4">
                      <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2">
                        <div>
                          <Label className="text-sm font-semibold">Budget Range</Label>
                          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                            ${parseFloat(requirement.budgetMin || "0").toLocaleString()} - $
                            {parseFloat(requirement.budgetMax || "0").toLocaleString()}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                          <Label className="text-sm font-semibold">Property Types</Label>
                          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                            {requirement.propertyTypes?.join(", ") || "Not specified"}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                          <Label className="text-sm font-semibold">Preferred Areas</Label>
                          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                            {requirement.preferredAreas?.join(", ") || "Not specified"}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                          <Label className="text-sm font-semibold">Bedrooms / Bathrooms</Label>
                          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                            {requirement.bedrooms} bed / {requirement.bathrooms} bath
                          </p>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                          <Label className="text-sm font-semibold">Urgency Level</Label>
                          <Badge variant="outline">{requirement.urgencyLevel}</Badge>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                          <Label className="text-sm font-semibold">Timeframe</Label>
                          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                            {requirement.timeframe?.replace("_", " ")}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                </TabsContent>

                {/* Property Matches Tab */}
                <TabsContent value="matches" className="space-y-4">
                  <Card>
                    <CardHeader>
                      <CardTitle>Scope Fit Scoring</CardTitle>
                      <CardDescription>
                        Properties ranked by overall match score with detailed scoring breakdown
                      </CardDescription>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent>
                      {propertyMatches.length === 0 ? (
                        <p className="text-center text-muted-foreground py-8">
                          No property matches found. Properties will be automatically matched based on requirements.
                        </p>
                      ) : (
                        <ScrollArea className="h-[600px]">
                          <div className="space-y-4">
                            {propertyMatches.map((match: any, index: number) => (
                              <Card key={match.id} className="border">
                                <CardContent className="pt-6">
                                  <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-4">
                                    <div>
                                      <h3 className="font-semibold text-lg" data-testid={`text-property-address-${index}`}>
                                        {match.property?.address || "Property Address"}
                                      </h3>
                                      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                                        {match.property?.city}, {match.property?.province}
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <Badge className={getMatchScoreColor(parseFloat(match.overallScore))} data-testid={`badge-match-score-${index}`}>
                                      {(parseFloat(match.overallScore) * 100).toFixed(0)}% Match
                                    </Badge>
                                  </div>

                                  {/* Score Breakdown */}
                                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-4">
                                    <div>
                                      <Label className="text-xs">Budget</Label>
                                      <Progress value={parseFloat(match.budgetScore || "0") * 100} className="h-2 mt-1" />
                                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                                        {(parseFloat(match.budgetScore || "0") * 100).toFixed(0)}%
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <div>
                                      <Label className="text-xs">Location</Label>
                                      <Progress value={parseFloat(match.locationScore || "0") * 100} className="h-2 mt-1" />
                                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                                        {(parseFloat(match.locationScore || "0") * 100).toFixed(0)}%
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <div>
                                      <Label className="text-xs">Size</Label>
                                      <Progress value={parseFloat(match.sizeScore || "0") * 100} className="h-2 mt-1" />
                                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                                        {(parseFloat(match.sizeScore || "0") * 100).toFixed(0)}%
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <div>
                                      <Label className="text-xs">Type</Label>
                                      <Progress value={parseFloat(match.typeScore || "0") * 100} className="h-2 mt-1" />
                                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                                        {(parseFloat(match.typeScore || "0") * 100).toFixed(0)}%
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <div>
                                      <Label className="text-xs">Amenities</Label>
                                      <Progress value={parseFloat(match.amenityScore || "0") * 100} className="h-2 mt-1" />
                                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                                        {(parseFloat(match.amenityScore || "0") * 100).toFixed(0)}%
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <div>
                                      <Label className="text-xs">Timeline</Label>
                                      <Progress value={parseFloat(match.timelineScore || "0") * 100} className="h-2 mt-1" />
                                      <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                                        {(parseFloat(match.timelineScore || "0") * 100).toFixed(0)}%
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                  </div>

                                  {/* Match Highlights & Deal Breakers */}
                                  <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                                    {match.highlights && match.highlights.length > 0 && (
                                      <div>
                                        <Label className="text-xs flex items-center gap-1">
                                          <CheckCircle className="h-3 w-3 text-green-600" />
                                          Highlights
                                        </Label>
                                        <ul className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1 space-y-1">
                                          {match.highlights.map((highlight: string, i: number) => (
                                            <li key={i}>• {highlight}</li>
                                          ))}
                                        </ul>
                                      </div>
                                    )}
                                    {match.dealBreakers && match.dealBreakers.length > 0 && (
                                      <div>
                                        <Label className="text-xs flex items-center gap-1">
                                          <XCircle className="h-3 w-3 text-red-600" />
                                          Deal Breakers
                                        </Label>
                                        <ul className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1 space-y-1">
                                          {match.dealBreakers.map((breaker: string, i: number) => (
                                            <li key={i}>• {breaker}</li>
                                          ))}
                                        </ul>
                                      </div>
                                    )}
                                  </div>

                                  {match.matchReason && (
                                    <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-4 italic">
                                      {match.matchReason}
                                    </p>
                                  )}
                                </CardContent>
                              </Card>
                            ))}
                          </div>
                        </ScrollArea>
                      )}
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                </TabsContent>

                {/* Exceptions Tab */}
                <TabsContent value="exceptions" className="space-y-4">
                  <Card>
                    <CardHeader>
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                        <div>
                          <CardTitle>Exceptions Register</CardTitle>
                          <CardDescription>
                            Special cases and requirement overrides for this client
                          </CardDescription>
                        </div>
                        <Button onClick={() => setShowExceptionModal(true)} data-testid="button-add-exception">
                          <Plus className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                          Add Exception
                        </Button>
                      </div>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent>
                      {exceptions.length === 0 ? (
                        <p className="text-center text-muted-foreground py-8">
                          No exceptions registered. Add exceptions for special circumstances.
                        </p>
                      ) : (
                        <div className="space-y-4">
                          {exceptions.map((exception: any, index: number) => (
                            <Card key={exception.id} className="border">
                              <CardContent className="pt-6">
                                <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-2">
                                  <Badge variant="outline" data-testid={`badge-exception-type-${index}`}>
                                    {exception.exceptionType?.replace(/_/g, " ")}
                                  </Badge>
                                  <Badge variant={exception.status === "approved" ? "default" : "secondary"}>
                                    {exception.status}
                                  </Badge>
                                </div>
                                <h4 className="font-semibold mb-2">{exception.description}</h4>
                                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-2">
                                  <strong>Justification:</strong> {exception.justification}
                                </p>
                                <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                                  <span>
                                    <Clock className="h-3 w-3 inline mr-1" />
                                    {format(new Date(exception.createdAt), "MMM d, yyyy")}
                                  </span>
                                  {exception.expiresAt && (
                                    <span>
                                      <Calendar className="h-3 w-3 inline mr-1" />
                                      Expires: {format(new Date(exception.expiresAt), "MMM d, yyyy")}
                                    </span>
                                  )}
                                </div>
                              </CardContent>
                            </Card>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                </TabsContent>

                {/* History Tab */}
                <TabsContent value="history" className="space-y-4">
                  <Card>
                    <CardHeader>
                      <CardTitle>Version History</CardTitle>
                      <CardDescription>
                        Complete audit trail of requirement changes and updates
                      </CardDescription>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent>
                      {versions.length === 0 ? (
                        <p className="text-center text-muted-foreground py-8">
                          No version history available.
                        </p>
                      ) : (
                        <div className="space-y-4">
                          {versions.map((version: any, index: number) => (
                            <div key={version.id} className="flex gap-4 border-l-2 pl-4 py-2">
                              <div className="flex-1">
                                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                                  <Badge variant="outline" data-testid={`badge-version-${index}`}>
                                    v{version.version}
                                  </Badge>
                                  <Badge>{version.changeType}</Badge>
                                </div>
                                {version.changeReason && (
                                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-1">
                                    {version.changeReason}
                                  </p>
                                )}
                                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                                  <Clock className="h-3 w-3 inline mr-1" />
                                  {format(new Date(version.createdAt), "MMM d, yyyy 'at' h:mm a")}
                                </p>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                </TabsContent>
              </Tabs>
            )}
          </>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Add Exception Modal */}
      <Dialog open={showExceptionModal} onOpenChange={setShowExceptionModal}>
        <DialogContent data-testid="modal-add-exception">
          <DialogHeader>
            <DialogTitle>Add Requirement Exception</DialogTitle>
            <DialogDescription>
              Create a special exception for this client's requirements
            </DialogDescription>
          </DialogHeader>
          <div className="space-y-4 py-4">
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="exception-type">Exception Type</Label>
              <Select value={exceptionType} onValueChange={setExceptionType}>
                <SelectTrigger id="exception-type" data-testid="select-exception-type">
                  <SelectValue placeholder="Select exception type" />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  <SelectItem value="budget_override">Budget Override</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="area_expansion">Area Expansion</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="criteria_waiver">Criteria Waiver</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="timeline_extension">Timeline Extension</SelectItem>
                  <SelectItem value="special_circumstance">Special Circumstance</SelectItem>
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="exception-description">Description</Label>
              <Input
                id="exception-description"
                value={exceptionDescription}
                onChange={(e) => setExceptionDescription(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Brief description of the exception"
                data-testid="input-exception-description"
              />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="exception-justification">Justification</Label>
              <Textarea
                id="exception-justification"
                value={exceptionJustification}
                onChange={(e) => setExceptionJustification(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Detailed justification for this exception"
                className="min-h-[100px]"
                data-testid="input-exception-justification"
              />
            </div>
          </div>
          <DialogFooter>
            <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowExceptionModal(false)} data-testid="button-cancel-exception">
              Cancel
            </Button>
            <Button
              onClick={handleCreateException}
              disabled={createExceptionMutation.isPending}
              data-testid="button-submit-exception"
            >
              {createExceptionMutation.isPending ? "Creating..." : "Create Exception"}
            </Button>
          </DialogFooter>
        </DialogContent>
      </Dialog>

      <MobileNav userRole={user?.role || "client"} />
    </div>
  );
}
```

## FILE: client/src/pages/ToursPage.tsx
```typescript
import { useState } from "react";
import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useAuth } from "@/hooks/useAuth";
import type { Tour } from "@shared/schema";
import Header from "@/components/Header";
import AgentSidebar from "@/components/AgentSidebar";
import { SidebarProvider, SidebarInset } from "@/components/ui/sidebar";
import TourWizardModal from "@/components/TourWizardModal";
import TourRecapModal from "@/components/TourRecapModal";
import ScheduleEditModal from "@/components/ScheduleEditModal";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Plus, Calendar, MapPin, Clock, Users, Route } from "lucide-react";
import { format } from "date-fns";

export default function ToursPage() {
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [showTourWizard, setShowTourWizard] = useState(false);
  const [showTourRecap, setShowTourRecap] = useState(false);
  const [showScheduleEdit, setShowScheduleEdit] = useState(false);
  const [selectedTour, setSelectedTour] = useState<Tour | null>(null);

  // Fetch tours for the agent
  const { data: tours = [], isLoading } = useQuery<Tour[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/tours"],
    enabled: !!user && user.role === 'agent',
  });

  const getStatusColor = (status: string) => {
    switch (status) {
      case 'scheduled': return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800';
      case 'in_progress': return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
      case 'completed': return 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800';
      case 'cancelled': return 'bg-red-100 text-red-800';
      default: return 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800';
    }
  };

  const handleEditTour = (tour: Tour) => {
    setSelectedTour(tour);
    setShowScheduleEdit(true);
  };

  const handleTourRecap = (tour: Tour) => {
    setSelectedTour(tour);
    setShowTourRecap(true);
  };

  if (!user) {
    return <div>Loading...</div>;
  }

  return (
    <SidebarProvider>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
        <Header userRole={user.role} />
        <div className="flex">
          <AgentSidebar />
          <SidebarInset>
            <main className="flex-1 p-6">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold">Tours & Scheduling</h1>
              <p className="text-muted-foreground">Manage your property tours and schedules</p>
            </div>
            <Button 
              onClick={() => setShowTourWizard(true)}
              className="gap-2"
              data-testid="button-new-tour"
            >
              <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
              New Tour
            </Button>
          </div>

          {isLoading ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
              <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-8 w-8 border-b-2 border-primary"></div>
            </div>
          ) : tours.length === 0 ? (
            <Card>
              <CardContent className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-12">
                <Calendar className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mb-4" />
                <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No tours scheduled</h3>
                <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center mb-4">
                  Create your first tour to get started with property showings.
                </p>
                <Button 
                  onClick={() => setShowTourWizard(true)}
                  className="gap-2"
                >
                  <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
                  Create First Tour
                </Button>
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
          ) : (
            <div className="grid gap-6">
              {tours.map((tour) => (
                <Card key={tour.id} className="hover:shadow-md transition-shadow">
                  <CardHeader>
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                      <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <Calendar className="h-5 w-5" />
                        Tour on {tour.scheduledDate ? format(new Date(tour.scheduledDate), 'MMM dd, yyyy') : 'Date TBD'}
                      </CardTitle>
                      <Badge className={getStatusColor(tour.status || 'requested')}>
                        {tour.status || 'requested'}
                      </Badge>
                    </div>
                  </CardHeader>
                  <CardContent>
                    <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                      <div className="space-y-2">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                          <Clock className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
                          {tour.startTime ? format(new Date(tour.startTime), 'h:mm a') : 'Time TBD'}
                        </div>
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                          <Users className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
                          Client Tour
                        </div>
                        {tour.totalDistance && (
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                            <Route className="h-4 w-4 text-muted-foreground" />
                            {tour.totalDistance} km total distance
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
                        <Button 
                          variant="outline" 
                          size="sm"
                          onClick={() => handleEditTour(tour)}
                          data-testid={`button-edit-tour-${tour.id}`}
                        >
                          Edit Schedule
                        </Button>
                        {tour.status === 'completed' && (
                          <Button 
                            variant="outline" 
                            size="sm"
                            onClick={() => handleTourRecap(tour)}
                            data-testid={`button-tour-recap-${tour.id}`}
                          >
                            View Recap
                          </Button>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    {tour.notes && (
                      <div className="mt-4 p-3 bg-muted rounded-md">
                        <p className="text-sm">{tour.notes}</p>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </CardContent>
                </Card>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
            </main>
          </SidebarInset>
        </div>
      </div>

      <TourWizardModal 
        isOpen={showTourWizard}
        onClose={() => setShowTourWizard(false)}
      />

      {selectedTour && selectedTour.scheduledDate && (
        <>
          <TourRecapModal
            isOpen={showTourRecap}
            onClose={() => {
              setShowTourRecap(false);
              setSelectedTour(null);
            }}
            selectedDate={new Date(selectedTour.scheduledDate)}
          />
          <ScheduleEditModal
            isOpen={showScheduleEdit}
            onClose={() => {
              setShowScheduleEdit(false);
              setSelectedTour(null);
            }}
            selectedDate={new Date(selectedTour.scheduledDate)}
          />
        </>
      )}
    </SidebarProvider>
  );
}```

## FILE: client/src/components/ClientProfileModal.tsx
```typescript
import { useState } from "react";
import { useQuery, useMutation } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useAuth } from "@/hooks/useAuth";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { apiRequest, queryClient } from "@/lib/queryClient";
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Avatar, AvatarFallback, AvatarImage } from "@/components/ui/avatar";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area";
import { 
  User,
  FileText,
  Eye,
  History,
  Heart,
  DollarSign,
  FolderOpen,
  Camera,
  StickyNote,
  Users,
  Calendar,
  MapPin,
  Phone,
  Mail,
  Briefcase,
  Home,
  Building2,
  Plus,
  Edit3,
  Trash2,
  Download,
  Upload,
  MessageCircle,
  Star,
  Clock,
  CheckCircle,
  XCircle,
  Target,
  TrendingUp,
  Shield,
  Zap
} from "lucide-react";
import RequirementsFormModal from "./RequirementsFormModal";
import { PropertyMediaGallery } from "./PropertyMediaGallery";
import { PropertyRatingModal } from "./PropertyRatingModal";

interface ClientProfileModalProps {
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  client: {
    id: string;
    firstName?: string;
    lastName?: string;
    email?: string;
    profileImageUrl?: string;
    clientType?: "buyer" | "renter";
    rentalProfile?: {
      propertyType: string;
      monthlyBudget: string;
      preferredAreas: string[];
      bedrooms: number;
      bathrooms: string;
    };
    stats?: {
      totalTours: number;
      shortlistedProperties: number;
      activeOffers: number;
      lastActivity: string;
    };
  };
}

export default function ClientProfileModal({ isOpen, onClose, client }: ClientProfileModalProps) {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const { user } = useAuth();
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("requirements");
  const [newNote, setNewNote] = useState("");
  const [showRequirementsForm, setShowRequirementsForm] = useState(false);
  const [selectedProperty, setSelectedProperty] = useState<any | null>(null);
  const [selectedTourId, setSelectedTourId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showRatingModal, setShowRatingModal] = useState(false);
  const [selectedPropertyForRating, setSelectedPropertyForRating] = useState<{
    propertyId: string;
    tourId: string;
  } | null>(null);

  // Fetch enhanced client requirements data
  const { data: clientRequirementsEnhanced, isLoading: requirementsLoading } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "requirements-enhanced"],
    enabled: isOpen && activeTab === "requirements",
  });

  const { data: clientHistory } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "history"],
    enabled: isOpen && activeTab === "history",
  });

  const { data: clientShortlists } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "shortlists"],
    enabled: isOpen && activeTab === "shortlists",
  });

  const { data: clientOffers } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "offers"],
    enabled: isOpen && activeTab === "offers",
  });

  const { data: clientDocuments } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "documents"],
    enabled: isOpen && activeTab === "documents",
  });

  const { data: clientMedia } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "media"],
    enabled: isOpen && activeTab === "media",
  });

  const { data: clientNotes } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "notes"],
    enabled: isOpen && activeTab === "notes",
  });

  const { data: clientGroups } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "groups"],
    enabled: isOpen && activeTab === "groups",
  });

  // Mutation for adding notes
  const addNoteMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (note: string) => {
      await apiRequest("POST", `/api/clients/${client.id}/notes`, { content: note });
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "notes"] });
      setNewNote("");
      toast({
        title: "Note Added",
        description: "Client note has been saved successfully.",
      });
    },
  });

  // Mutation for deleting client
  const deleteClientMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async () => {
      await apiRequest("DELETE", `/api/clients/${client.id}`);
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["/api/clients"] });
      toast({
        title: "Client Deleted",
        description: "Client has been removed successfully.",
      });
      onClose();
    },
    onError: () => {
      toast({
        title: "Error",
        description: "Failed to delete client. Please try again.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    },
  });

  const handleAddNote = () => {
    if (newNote.trim()) {
      addNoteMutation.mutate(newNote.trim());
    }
  };

  const formatDate = (dateString: string) => {
    return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString();
  };

  const formatCurrency = (amount: string | number) => {
    return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-CA', { 
      style: 'currency', 
      currency: 'CAD' 
    }).format(Number(amount));
  };

  return (
    <Dialog open={isOpen} onOpenChange={onClose}>
      <DialogContent className="max-w-6xl h-[90vh] p-0" data-testid="dialog-client-profile">
        <div className="flex flex-col h-full">
          {/* Header */}
          <DialogHeader className="p-6 border-b border-border">
            <div className="flex items-center space-x-4">
              <Avatar className="h-16 w-16">
                <AvatarImage 
                  src={client.profileImageUrl || ""} 
                  alt={`${client.firstName} ${client.lastName}`} 
                />
                <AvatarFallback className="text-lg">
                  {client.firstName?.[0]}{client.lastName?.[0]}
                </AvatarFallback>
              </Avatar>
              <div className="flex-1">
                <DialogTitle className="text-2xl mb-2" data-testid="text-client-profile-name">
                  {client.firstName} {client.lastName}
                </DialogTitle>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                  <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                    <Mail className="h-4 w-4" />
                    {client.email}
                  </span>
                  {client.clientType && (
                    <Badge variant="outline" data-testid="badge-client-type">
                      {client.clientType === "buyer" ? "Buyer" : "Renter"}
                    </Badge>
                  )}
                  <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                    <Calendar className="h-4 w-4" />
                    Last Activity: {client.stats?.lastActivity ? formatDate(client.stats.lastActivity) : "Never"}
                  </span>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-2">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-sm">
                  <div className="text-center">
                    <p className="font-semibold text-lg">{client.stats?.totalTours || 0}</p>
                    <p className="text-muted-foreground">Tours</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-center">
                    <p className="font-semibold text-lg">{client.stats?.shortlistedProperties || 0}</p>
                    <p className="text-muted-foreground">Shortlisted</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-center">
                    <p className="font-semibold text-lg">{client.stats?.activeOffers || 0}</p>
                    <p className="text-muted-foreground">Offers</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <Button size="sm" variant="outline" onClick={() => {
                    toast({
                      title: "Edit Client",
                      description: "Edit functionality coming soon.",
                    });
                  }} data-testid="button-edit-client">
                    <Edit3 className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                    Edit
                  </Button>
                  <Button size="sm" variant="destructive" onClick={() => {
                    if (confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete ${client.firstName} ${client.lastName}? This action cannot be undone.`)) {
                      deleteClientMutation.mutate();
                    }
                  }} data-testid="button-delete-client">
                    <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                    Delete
                  </Button>
                  <Button size="sm" data-testid="button-message-client">
                    <MessageCircle className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                    Message
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </DialogHeader>

          {/* Tab Navigation */}
          <Tabs value={activeTab} onValueChange={setActiveTab} className="flex-1 flex flex-col">
            <div className="border-b border-border px-6">
              <TabsList className="grid w-full grid-cols-9 bg-transparent h-12">
                <TabsTrigger value="requirements" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-requirements">
                  <User className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Requirements
                </TabsTrigger>
                <TabsTrigger value="transparency" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-transparency">
                  <Eye className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Transparency
                </TabsTrigger>
                <TabsTrigger value="history" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-history">
                  <History className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  History
                </TabsTrigger>
                <TabsTrigger value="shortlists" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-shortlists">
                  <Heart className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Shortlists
                </TabsTrigger>
                <TabsTrigger value="offers" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-offers">
                  <DollarSign className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Offers
                </TabsTrigger>
                <TabsTrigger value="documents" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-documents">
                  <FolderOpen className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Documents
                </TabsTrigger>
                <TabsTrigger value="media" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-media">
                  <Camera className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Media
                </TabsTrigger>
                <TabsTrigger value="notes" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-notes">
                  <StickyNote className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Notes
                </TabsTrigger>
                <TabsTrigger value="groups" className="data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-primary-foreground" data-testid="tab-groups">
                  <Users className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                  Groups
                </TabsTrigger>
              </TabsList>
            </div>

            {/* Tab Content */}
            <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
              <ScrollArea className="h-full">
                <div className="p-6">
                  
                  {/* Requirements Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="requirements" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <Card>
                        <CardHeader className="flex flex-row items-center justify-between space-y-0 pb-4">
                          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <Target className="h-5 w-5" />
                            {client.clientType === "buyer" ? "Buyer Requirements Profile" : "Rental Requirements Profile"}
                          </CardTitle>
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            {clientRequirementsEnhanced?.requirement && (
                              <Badge variant={
                                clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.status === 'validated' ? "default" :
                                clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.status === 'pending_validation' ? "secondary" : "outline"
                              }>
                                {clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.status.replace('_', ' ')}
                              </Badge>
                            )}
                            <Button 
                              size="sm" 
                              onClick={() => setShowRequirementsForm(true)}
                              data-testid="button-add-requirements"
                            >
                              <Plus className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                              {clientRequirementsEnhanced?.requirement ? 'Update Requirements' : 'Create Requirements'}
                            </Button>
                          </div>
                        </CardHeader>
                        <CardContent>
                          {requirementsLoading ? (
                            <div className="text-center py-8">
                              <Clock className="h-8 w-8 animate-spin mx-auto mb-4 text-muted-foreground" />
                              <p className="text-muted-foreground">Loading requirements...</p>
                            </div>
                          ) : clientRequirementsEnhanced?.requirement ? (
                            <div className="space-y-6">
                              {/* Validation Score Section */}
                              <div className="p-4 border rounded-lg bg-muted/50">
                                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
                                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                    <Shield className="h-4 w-4" />
                                    <h4 className="font-semibold">Requirements Validation</h4>
                                  </div>
                                  <Badge variant={
                                    Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.validationScore) >= 0.8 ? "default" :
                                    Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.validationScore) >= 0.5 ? "secondary" : "destructive"
                                  }>
                                    {(Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.validationScore) * 100).toFixed(0)}% Complete
                                  </Badge>
                                </div>
                                <div className="mb-3">
                                  <div className="flex justify-between text-sm mb-1">
                                    <span>Validation Score</span>
                                    <span className="font-medium">
                                      {(Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.validationScore) * 100).toFixed(0)}%
                                    </span>
                                  </div>
                                  <div className="w-full bg-secondary rounded-full h-2">
                                    <div 
                                      className={`h-2 rounded-full transition-all ${
                                        Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.validationScore) >= 0.8 ? 'bg-green-500' :
                                        Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.validationScore) >= 0.5 ? 'bg-yellow-500' : 'bg-red-500'
                                      }`}
                                      style={{ width: `${Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.validationScore) * 100}%` }}
                                    />
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                                <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                                  Last validated: {clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.lastValidatedAt 
                                    ? new Date(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.lastValidatedAt).toLocaleDateString() 
                                    : 'Never'}
                                </div>
                              </div>

                              {/* Core Requirements Display */}
                              <div className="space-y-4">
                                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4">
                                  <FileText className="h-4 w-4" />
                                  <h4 className="font-semibold">Requirements Summary</h4>
                                  <Badge variant="outline" className="ml-auto">
                                    v{clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.version}
                                  </Badge>
                                </div>
                                
                                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                                  <div className="p-3 border rounded-lg">
                                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                                      <DollarSign className="h-4 w-4 text-green-600" />
                                      <h5 className="font-medium">Budget Range</h5>
                                    </div>
                                    <p className="text-sm">
                                      ${Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.budgetMin).toLocaleString()} - 
                                      ${Number(clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.budgetMax).toLocaleString()}
                                    </p>
                                  </div>

                                  <div className="p-3 border rounded-lg">
                                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                                      <Home className="h-4 w-4 text-blue-600" />
                                      <h5 className="font-medium">Property Specs</h5>
                                    </div>
                                    <p className="text-sm">
                                      {clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.bedrooms} bed, {clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.bathrooms} bath
                                    </p>
                                  </div>

                                  <div className="p-3 border rounded-lg">
                                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                                      <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 text-purple-600" />
                                      <h5 className="font-medium">Preferred Areas</h5>
                                    </div>
                                    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                                      {clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.preferredAreas?.slice(0, 3).map((area: string) => (
                                        <Badge key={area} variant="secondary" className="text-xs">
                                          {area}
                                        </Badge>
                                      ))}
                                      {clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.preferredAreas?.length > 3 && (
                                        <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs">
                                          +{clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.preferredAreas.length - 3} more
                                        </Badge>
                                      )}
                                    </div>
                                  </div>

                                  <div className="p-3 border rounded-lg">
                                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                                      <Clock className="h-4 w-4 text-orange-600" />
                                      <h5 className="font-medium">Timeline</h5>
                                    </div>
                                    <div className="space-y-1">
                                      <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs">
                                        {clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.urgencyLevel} urgency
                                      </Badge>
                                      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                                        {clientRequirementsEnhanced.requirement.timeframe.replace('_', ' ')}
                                      </p>
                                    </div>
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          ) : (
                            <div className="text-center py-12">
                              <Target className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-4 text-muted-foreground" />
                              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-2">No Requirements Profile</h3>
                              <p className="text-muted-foreground mb-6 max-w-md mx-auto">
                                Create a comprehensive requirements profile to unlock property matching, validation scoring, and personalized recommendations.
                              </p>
                              <Button 
                                onClick={() => setShowRequirementsForm(true)}
                                data-testid="button-create-requirements-empty"
                                className="min-w-[160px]"
                              >
                                <Plus className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                                Create Requirements
                              </Button>
                            </div>
                          )}
                        </CardContent>
                      </Card>
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                  {/* Transparency Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="transparency" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <Card>
                        <CardHeader>
                          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <Eye className="h-5 w-5" />
                            Client Transparency Panel
                          </CardTitle>
                        </CardHeader>
                        <CardContent>
                          <div className="space-y-4">
                            <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border rounded-lg">
                              <div>
                                <h3 className="font-semibold">Requirements Completed</h3>
                                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Client has provided all necessary information</p>
                              </div>
                              <CheckCircle className="h-6 w-6 text-green-500" />
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border rounded-lg">
                              <div>
                                <h3 className="font-semibold">Background Check Consent</h3>
                                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Permission for background verification</p>
                              </div>
                              <XCircle className="h-6 w-6 text-red-500" />
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border rounded-lg">
                              <div>
                                <h3 className="font-semibold">Financial Pre-Approval</h3>
                                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Mortgage or income verification status</p>
                              </div>
                              <Clock className="h-6 w-6 text-yellow-500" />
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </CardContent>
                      </Card>
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                  {/* History Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="history" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      {clientHistory?.summary && (
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                          <Card>
                            <CardContent className="p-4">
                              <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{clientHistory.summary.totalTours}</div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Total Tours</div>
                            </CardContent>
                          </Card>
                          <Card>
                            <CardContent className="p-4">
                              <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{clientHistory.summary.totalPropertiesViewed}</div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Properties Viewed</div>
                            </CardContent>
                          </Card>
                          <Card>
                            <CardContent className="p-4">
                              <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{clientHistory.summary.totalRatings}</div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Properties Rated</div>
                            </CardContent>
                          </Card>
                          <Card>
                            <CardContent className="p-4">
                              <div className="text-2xl font-bold">{clientHistory.summary.totalOffers}</div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Offers Made</div>
                            </CardContent>
                          </Card>
                        </div>
                      )}

                      {/* Tours with Properties */}
                      {clientHistory?.tours?.map((tour: any) => (
                        <Card key={tour.id} data-testid={`tour-card-${tour.id}`}>
                          <CardHeader>
                            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                                <Calendar className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-600" />
                                <div>
                                  <CardTitle className="text-lg">
                                    {formatDate(tour.scheduledDate)}
                                  </CardTitle>
                                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                                    {tour.totalProperties} {tour.totalProperties === 1 ? 'property' : 'properties'} • {tour.status}
                                  </p>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              <Badge variant={tour.status === 'completed' ? 'default' : 'secondary'} data-testid={`tour-status-${tour.id}`}>
                                {tour.status}
                              </Badge>
                            </div>
                          </CardHeader>
                          <CardContent>
                            <div className="space-y-4">
                              {tour.properties?.map((property: any) => (
                                <div
                                  key={property.id}
                                  className="p-4 border rounded-lg hover:bg-accent/50 transition-colors cursor-pointer"
                                  data-testid={`property-card-${property.id}`}
                                  onClick={() => {
                                    setSelectedProperty(property);
                                    setSelectedTourId(tour.id);
                                  }}
                                >
                                  <div className="flex gap-4">
                                    {property.imageUrl ? (
                                      <img
                                        src={property.imageUrl}
                                        alt={property.address}
                                        className="w-24 h-24 object-cover rounded"
                                      />
                                    ) : (
                                      <div className="w-24 h-24 bg-gray-200 rounded flex items-center justify-center">
                                        <Home className="h-8 w-8 text-gray-400" />
                                      </div>
                                    )}
                                    <div className="flex-1">
                                      <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-2">
                                        <div>
                                          <h4 className="font-semibold" data-testid={`property-address-${property.id}`}>
                                            {property.address}
                                          </h4>
                                          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                                            {property.bedrooms} bed • {property.bathrooms} bath • ${Number(property.price).toLocaleString()}
                                          </p>
                                        </div>
                                        {property.rating && (
                                          <div className="flex items-center gap-1" data-testid={`property-rating-${property.id}`}>
                                            {[...Array(5)].map((_, i) => (
                                              <Star
                                                key={i}
                                                className={`h-4 w-4 ${
                                                  i < property.rating.rating
                                                    ? 'fill-yellow-400 text-yellow-400'
                                                    : 'text-gray-300'
                                                }`}
                                              />
                                            ))}
                                          </div>
                                        )}
                                      </div>

                                      {/* Feedback */}
                                      {property.rating && (
                                        <div className="mt-3 p-3 bg-muted/50 rounded-lg" data-testid={`property-feedback-${property.id}`}>
                                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
