                                            {property.rating.feedbackCategory === 'offer_now' && (
                                              <>
                                                <Badge className="bg-green-100 text-green-800">Offer Now</Badge>
                                                <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{property.rating.reason}</span>
                                              </>
                                            )}
                                            {property.rating.feedbackCategory === 'hold_later' && (
                                              <>
                                                <Badge className="bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800">Hold</Badge>
                                                <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{property.rating.reason}</span>
                                              </>
                                            )}
                                            {property.rating.feedbackCategory === 'reject' && (
                                              <>
                                                <Badge className="bg-red-100 text-red-800">Reject</Badge>
                                                <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{property.rating.reason}</span>
                                              </>
                                            )}
                                          </div>
                                          {property.rating.notes && (
                                            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground italic">
                                              "{property.rating.notes}"
                                            </p>
                                          )}
                                        </div>
                                      )}

                                      {/* Action Buttons */}
                                      <div className="mt-3 flex gap-2">
                                        {!property.rating && (
                                          <Button
                                            size="sm"
                                            variant="outline"
                                            className="text-xs"
                                            data-testid={`button-rate-property-${property.id}`}
                                            onClick={(e) => {
                                              e.stopPropagation();
                                              setSelectedPropertyForRating({
                                                propertyId: property.id,
                                                tourId: tour.id
                                              });
                                              setShowRatingModal(true);
                                            }}
                                          >
                                            <Star className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                                            Rate Property
                                          </Button>
                                        )}
                                        <Button
                                          size="sm"
                                          variant="ghost"
                                          className="text-xs"
                                          data-testid={`button-view-details-${property.id}`}
                                          onClick={(e) => {
                                            e.stopPropagation();
                                            setSelectedProperty(property);
                                            setSelectedTourId(tour.id);
                                          }}
                                        >
                                          <Eye className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
                                          View Details & Media
                                        </Button>
                                      </div>
                                    </div>
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                              ))}
                            </div>
                          </CardContent>
                        </Card>
                      ))}

                      {/* Empty State */}
                      {(!clientHistory?.tours || clientHistory.tours.length === 0) && (
                        <Card>
                          <CardContent className="text-center py-12">
                            <History className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-4 text-muted-foreground" />
                            <h3 className="font-semibold mb-2">No Tour History</h3>
                            <p className="text-muted-foreground">
                              This client hasn't toured any properties yet.
                            </p>
                          </CardContent>
                        </Card>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                  {/* Shortlists Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="shortlists" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <Card>
                        <CardHeader>
                          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <Heart className="h-5 w-5" />
                            Shortlisted Properties
                          </CardTitle>
                        </CardHeader>
                        <CardContent>
                          <div className="text-center py-8">
                            <Heart className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No Properties Shortlisted</h3>
                            <p className="text-muted-foreground">Client hasn't shortlisted any properties yet.</p>
                          </div>
                        </CardContent>
                      </Card>
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                  {/* Offers Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="offers" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <Card>
                        <CardHeader>
                          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <DollarSign className="h-5 w-5" />
                            Offers & Applications
                          </CardTitle>
                        </CardHeader>
                        <CardContent>
                          <div className="text-center py-8">
                            <DollarSign className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No Active Offers</h3>
                            <p className="text-muted-foreground">Client hasn't submitted any offers yet.</p>
                          </div>
                        </CardContent>
                      </Card>
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                  {/* Documents Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="documents" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <Card>
                        <CardHeader>
                          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <FolderOpen className="h-5 w-5" />
                            Client Documents
                          </CardTitle>
                        </CardHeader>
                        <CardContent>
                          <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">
                            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Manage client documents and forms</p>
                            <Button size="sm">
                              <Upload className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
                              Upload Document
                            </Button>
                          </div>
                          <div className="text-center py-8">
                            <FolderOpen className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No Documents</h3>
                            <p className="text-muted-foreground">No documents have been uploaded yet.</p>
                          </div>
                        </CardContent>
                      </Card>
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                  {/* Media Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="media" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <Card>
                        <CardHeader>
                          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <Camera className="h-5 w-5" />
                            Media & Photos
                          </CardTitle>
                        </CardHeader>
                        <CardContent>
                          <div className="text-center py-8">
                            <Camera className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No Media Files</h3>
                            <p className="text-muted-foreground">Property photos and videos will appear here.</p>
                          </div>
                        </CardContent>
                      </Card>
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                  {/* Notes Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="notes" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <Card>
                        <CardHeader>
                          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <StickyNote className="h-5 w-5" />
                            Agent Notes
                          </CardTitle>
                        </CardHeader>
                        <CardContent>
                          <div className="space-y-4">
                            <div className="flex gap-2">
                              <Textarea
                                placeholder="Add a note about this client..."
                                value={newNote}
                                onChange={(e) => setNewNote(e.target.value)}
                                className="flex-1"
                                data-testid="textarea-new-note"
                              />
                              <Button 
                                onClick={handleAddNote}
                                disabled={!newNote.trim() || addNoteMutation.isPending}
                                data-testid="button-add-note"
                              >
                                <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
                              </Button>
                            </div>
                            
                            <div className="space-y-3">
                              {[
                                { date: "2024-01-15", content: "Client prefers ground floor units due to mobility concerns.", author: "Agent" },
                                { date: "2024-01-12", content: "Very interested in properties with parking. Will pay premium for secured parking.", author: "Agent" },
                                { date: "2024-01-10", content: "Client is pre-approved for up to $500k. Looking to move by March.", author: "Agent" },
                              ].map((note, index) => (
                                <div key={index} className="p-4 border rounded-lg bg-muted/30">
                                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                                    <span className="text-sm font-medium">{note.author}</span>
                                    <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{formatDate(note.date)}</span>
                                  </div>
                                  <p className="text-sm">{note.content}</p>
                                </div>
                              ))}
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </CardContent>
                      </Card>
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                  {/* Groups Tab */}
                  <TabsContent value="groups" className="m-0">
                    <div className="space-y-6">
                      <Card>
                        <CardHeader>
                          <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <Users className="h-5 w-5" />
                            Client Groups
                          </CardTitle>
                        </CardHeader>
                        <CardContent>
                          <div className="text-center py-8">
                            <Users className="h-12 w-12 text-muted-foreground mx-auto mb-4" />
                            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">No Groups</h3>
                            <p className="text-muted-foreground">Client is not part of any collaboration groups.</p>
                          </div>
                        </CardContent>
                      </Card>
                    </div>
                  </TabsContent>

                </div>
              </ScrollArea>
            </div>
          </Tabs>
        </div>
      </DialogContent>

      {/* Requirements Form Modal */}
      <RequirementsFormModal
        isOpen={showRequirementsForm}
        onClose={() => setShowRequirementsForm(false)}
        client={client}
      />

      {/* Property Media Gallery Modal */}
      {selectedProperty && selectedTourId && (
        <PropertyMediaGallery
          open={!!selectedProperty}
          onOpenChange={(open) => {
            if (!open) {
              setSelectedProperty(null);
              setSelectedTourId(null);
            }
          }}
          propertyId={selectedProperty.id}
          tourId={selectedTourId}
          property={selectedProperty}
          rating={selectedProperty.rating}
        />
      )}

      {/* Property Rating Modal (for agents to rate on behalf of clients) */}
      {selectedPropertyForRating && (
        <PropertyRatingModal
          isOpen={showRatingModal}
          onClose={() => {
            setShowRatingModal(false);
            setSelectedPropertyForRating(null);
            // Refresh client history after rating
            queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["/api/clients", client.id, "history"] });
          }}
          propertyId={selectedPropertyForRating.propertyId}
          tourId={selectedPropertyForRating.tourId}
        />
      )}
    </Dialog>
  );
}```

## FILE: client/src/components/PropertyRatingModal.tsx
```typescript
import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { useMutation, useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { apiRequest, queryClient } from "@/lib/queryClient";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
  DialogDescription,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
import {
  Select,
  SelectContent,
  SelectItem,
  SelectTrigger,
  SelectValue,
} from "@/components/ui/select";
import { Checkbox } from "@/components/ui/checkbox";
import { Star, CheckCircle2, Clock, XCircle } from "lucide-react";

interface PropertyRatingModalProps {
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  propertyId: string;
  tourId: string;
  propertyAddress: string;
}

// Comprehensive feedback categories with all 36 reasons (per specification)
const FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES = {
  offer_now: {
    label: "Acceptance – Float an Offer",
    icon: CheckCircle2,
    color: "text-green-600",
    reasons: [
      "Meets all needs",
      "Great location",
      "Ideal price/value",
      "Excellent condition/renovated",
      "Strong investment potential",
      "Layout is perfect",
      "Quiet street/neighbourhood",
      "Close to work/school/transit",
      "Move-in ready",
      "Superior lot/outdoor space",
      "Building amenities fit lifestyle",
      "Competitive market advantage",
    ],
  },
  hold_later: {
    label: "Acceptance – Park for Future Offer",
    icon: Clock,
    color: "text-yellow-600",
    reasons: [
      "Compare with other options",
      "Need partner/family alignment",
      "Seek better price/terms",
      "Financing in progress",
      "Awaiting inspection details",
      "Timing not urgent",
      "Re-visit at different time/day",
      "Watch for price adjustment",
      "Check condo/HOA details",
      "Verify neighbourhood trends",
      "Pending sale of current home",
      "Awaiting status documents",
    ],
  },
  reject: {
    label: "Rejection – No Offer",
    icon: XCircle,
    color: "text-red-600",
    reasons: [
      "Over budget",
      "Poor layout",
      "Location not preferred",
      "Needs too much work",
      "Too small/insufficient space",
      "Missing must-have feature(s)",
      "Commute inconvenient",
      "Fees/taxes too high",
      "No outdoor space/parking",
      "Building/area vibe not a fit",
      "Insufficient natural light",
      "Noise or privacy concerns",
    ],
  },
};

export function PropertyRatingModal({
  isOpen,
  onClose,
  propertyId,
  tourId,
  propertyAddress,
}: PropertyRatingModalProps) {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const [rating, setRating] = useState(0);
  const [hoveredRating, setHoveredRating] = useState(0);
  const [feedbackCategory, setFeedbackCategory] = useState<string>("");
  const [reason, setReason] = useState<string>("");
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState<string>("");
  const [remindLater, setRemindLater] = useState(false);

  // Fetch existing rating
  const { data: existingRating, isLoading, isError } = useQuery<any>({
    queryKey: [`/api/tours/${tourId}/properties/${propertyId}/rating`],
    enabled: isOpen && !!tourId && !!propertyId,
  });

  // Pre-fill form if rating exists
  useEffect(() => {
    if (existingRating) {
      setRating(existingRating.rating || 0);
      setFeedbackCategory(existingRating.feedbackCategory || "");
      setReason(existingRating.reason || "");
      setNotes(existingRating.notes || "");
      setRemindLater(existingRating.remindLater || false);
    } else {
      // Reset form when no existing rating
      setRating(0);
      setFeedbackCategory("");
      setReason("");
      setNotes("");
      setRemindLater(false);
    }
  }, [existingRating, isOpen]);

  // Save rating mutation
  const saveRatingMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (data: any) => {
      const response = await apiRequest(
        "POST",
        `/api/tours/${tourId}/properties/${propertyId}/rating`,
        data
      );
      return response.json();
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: [`/api/tours/${tourId}/properties/${propertyId}/rating`] });
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: [`/api/tours/${tourId}/ratings`] });
      toast({
        title: "Rating Saved",
        description: "Your property rating has been saved successfully.",
      });
      onClose();
    },
    onError: (error: any) => {
      toast({
        title: "Error",
        description: error.message || "Failed to save rating. Please try again.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    },
  });

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    // Validation
    if (rating === 0) {
      toast({
        title: "Rating Required",
        description: "Please select a star rating.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
      return;
    }

    if (!remindLater) {
      if (!feedbackCategory) {
        toast({
          title: "Feedback Required",
          description: "Please select a feedback category.",
          variant: "destructive",
        });
        return;
      }

      if (!reason) {
        toast({
          title: "Reason Required",
          description: "Please select a reason for your feedback.",
          variant: "destructive",
        });
        return;
      }
    }

    saveRatingMutation.mutate({
      rating,
      feedbackCategory: feedbackCategory || null,
      reason: reason || "Remind me later",
      notes: notes.trim() || null,
      remindLater,
    });
  };

  const handleRemindLater = () => {
    setRemindLater(!remindLater);
    if (!remindLater) {
      // When enabling remind later, clear category and reason
      setFeedbackCategory("");
      setReason("");
    }
  };

  const CategoryIcon = feedbackCategory ? FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES[feedbackCategory as keyof typeof FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES]?.icon : null;
  const categoryColor = feedbackCategory ? FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES[feedbackCategory as keyof typeof FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES]?.color : "";

  return (
    <Dialog open={isOpen} onOpenChange={onClose}>
      <DialogContent className="max-w-lg" data-testid="modal-property-rating">
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle>Rate Property</DialogTitle>
          <DialogDescription className="text-sm">
            {propertyAddress} - Please provide your feedback on this property
          </DialogDescription>
        </DialogHeader>

        {isLoading ? (
          <div className="py-8 text-center">
            <p className="text-muted-foreground">Loading...</p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <>
            {isError && (
              <div className="px-4 py-2 bg-destructive/10 text-destructive text-sm rounded">
                Failed to load existing rating. You can still submit a new rating below.
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="space-y-6">
            {/* Star Rating */}
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label>Rate this property *</Label>
              <div className="flex gap-2">
                {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((star) => (
                  <button
                    key={star}
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setRating(star)}
                    onMouseEnter={() => setHoveredRating(star)}
                    onMouseLeave={() => setHoveredRating(0)}
                    className="focus:outline-none transition-transform hover:scale-110"
                    data-testid={`star-${star}`}
                  >
                    <Star
                      className={`h-10 w-10 ${
                        star <= (hoveredRating || rating)
                          ? "fill-yellow-400 text-yellow-400"
                          : "text-gray-300"
                      }`}
                    />
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
              {rating > 0 && (
                <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                  {rating} star{rating !== 1 ? "s" : ""}
                </p>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Remind Me Later Option */}
            <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
              <Checkbox
                id="remind-later"
                checked={remindLater}
                onCheckedChange={handleRemindLater}
                data-testid="checkbox-remind-later"
              />
              <Label
                htmlFor="remind-later"
                className="text-sm font-normal cursor-pointer"
              >
                Remind me later to provide feedback
              </Label>
            </div>

            {!remindLater && (
              <>
                {/* Feedback Category */}
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label>Feedback Category *</Label>
                  <Select
                    value={feedbackCategory}
                    onValueChange={(value) => {
                      setFeedbackCategory(value);
                      setReason(""); // Reset reason when category changes
                    }}
                  >
                    <SelectTrigger data-testid="select-feedback-category">
                      <SelectValue placeholder="Select feedback category" />
                    </SelectTrigger>
                    <SelectContent>
                      {Object.entries(FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES).map(([key, cat]) => {
                        const Icon = cat.icon;
                        return (
                          <SelectItem key={key} value={key}>
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                              <Icon className={`h-4 w-4 ${cat.color}`} />
                              {cat.label}
                            </div>
                          </SelectItem>
                        );
                      })}
                    </SelectContent>
                  </Select>
                </div>

                {/* Reason */}
                {feedbackCategory && (
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    <Label>Reason *</Label>
                    <Select value={reason} onValueChange={setReason}>
                      <SelectTrigger data-testid="select-reason">
                        <SelectValue placeholder="Select a reason" />
                      </SelectTrigger>
                      <SelectContent>
                        {FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES[feedbackCategory as keyof typeof FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES]?.reasons.map(
                          (r) => (
                            <SelectItem key={r} value={r}>
                              {r}
                            </SelectItem>
                          )
                        )}
                      </SelectContent>
                    </Select>
                  </div>
                )}
              </>
            )}

            {/* Additional Notes */}
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <Label htmlFor="notes">Additional Notes (Optional)</Label>
              <Textarea
                id="notes"
                value={notes}
                onChange={(e) => setNotes(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Add any additional comments..."
                className="min-h-[100px] resize-none"
                data-testid="input-notes"
              />
            </div>

            {/* Action Buttons */}
            <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
              <Button
                variant="outline"
                onClick={onClose}
                disabled={saveRatingMutation.isPending}
                data-testid="button-cancel"
              >
                Cancel
              </Button>
              <Button
                onClick={handleSubmit}
                disabled={saveRatingMutation.isPending}
                data-testid="button-submit"
              >
                {saveRatingMutation.isPending ? "Saving..." : "Save Rating"}
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
          </>
        )}
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```

## FILE: client/src/components/PropertyMediaGallery.tsx
```typescript
import { useState } from "react";
import { useQuery, useMutation } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
import { Card, CardContent } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
import { Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue } from "@/components/ui/select";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { Star, Upload, FileText, Video, Image as ImageIcon, Trash2, Eye } from "lucide-react";
import { apiRequest, queryClient } from "@/lib/queryClient";
import type { PropertyMedia, PropertyRating } from "@shared/schema";

const FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES = {
  offer_now: { label: "Float Offer", emoji: "🏠", color: "bg-green-100 text-green-800" },
  hold_later: { label: "Park for Future", emoji: "🅿️", color: "bg-blue-100 text-blue-800" },
  reject: { label: "Reject", emoji: "❌", color: "bg-red-100 text-red-800" }
};

interface PropertyMediaGalleryProps {
  open: boolean;
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
  propertyId: string;
  tourId: string;
  property: any;
  rating?: PropertyRating;
}

export function PropertyMediaGallery({
  open,
  onOpenChange,
  propertyId,
  tourId,
  property,
  rating
}: PropertyMediaGalleryProps) {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);
  const [mediaType, setMediaType] = useState<"photo" | "video" | "document">("photo");
  const [documentType, setDocumentType] = useState<string>("other");
  const [caption, setCaption] = useState("");
  const [description, setDescription] = useState("");

  // Fetch property media
  const { data: media = [], isLoading } = useQuery<PropertyMedia[]>({
    queryKey: [`/api/properties/${propertyId}/tours/${tourId}/media`],
    enabled: open,
  });

  // Upload mutation
  const uploadMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (formData: FormData) => {
      const response = await fetch(`/api/properties/${propertyId}/tours/${tourId}/media`, {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData,
        credentials: 'include',
      });
      if (!response.ok) {
        const error = await response.json();
        throw new Error(error.message || 'Upload failed');
      }
      return response.json();
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: [`/api/properties/${propertyId}/tours/${tourId}/media`] });
      toast({
        title: "Upload successful",
        description: "Media has been uploaded successfully",
      });
      setCaption("");
      setDescription("");
    },
    onError: (error: Error) => {
      toast({
        title: "Upload failed",
        description: error.message,
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    },
  });

  // Delete mutation
  const deleteMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (mediaId: string) => {
      const response = await fetch(`/api/media/${mediaId}`, {
        method: 'DELETE',
        credentials: 'include',
      });
      if (!response.ok) {
        const error = await response.json();
        throw new Error(error.message || 'Delete failed');
      }
      return response.json();
    },
    onSuccess: () => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: [`/api/properties/${propertyId}/tours/${tourId}/media`] });
      toast({
        title: "Deleted",
        description: "Media has been deleted successfully",
      });
    },
  });

  const handleFileUpload = async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const files = e.target.files;
    if (!files || files.length === 0) return;

    // Check file limit
    if (media.length + files.length > 15) {
      toast({
        title: "Upload limit exceeded",
        description: "Maximum 15 files allowed per property viewing",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
      return;
    }

    setUploading(true);

    for (const file of Array.from(files)) {
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('file', file);
      formData.append('mediaType', mediaType);
      formData.append('documentType', documentType);
      formData.append('caption', caption);
      formData.append('description', description);

      try {
        await uploadMutation.mutateAsync(formData);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Upload error:', error);
      }
    }

    setUploading(false);
    e.target.value = '';
  };

  const photos = media.filter(m => m.mediaType === 'photo');
  const videos = media.filter(m => m.mediaType === 'video');
  const documents = media.filter(m => m.mediaType === 'document');

  return (
    <Dialog open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
      <DialogContent className="max-w-4xl max-h-[90vh] overflow-y-auto">
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle className="text-xl font-bold">
            {property.address}
          </DialogTitle>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            {property.bedrooms} bed · {property.bathrooms} bath · ${property.price?.toLocaleString()}
          </p>
        </DialogHeader>

        {/* Rating Section */}
        {rating && (
          <Card className="border-2">
            <CardContent className="p-4">
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <div className="flex items-center space-x-2 mb-2">
                    <div className="flex">
                      {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((star) => (
                        <Star
                          key={star}
                          className={`h-5 w-5 ${
                            star <= rating.rating
                              ? "fill-yellow-400 text-yellow-400"
                              : "text-gray-300"
                          }`}
                        />
                      ))}
                    </div>
                    <span className="font-semibold text-lg">{rating.rating}.0</span>
                  </div>
                  <Badge className={FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES[rating.feedbackCategory as keyof typeof FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES].color}>
                    {FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES[rating.feedbackCategory as keyof typeof FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES].emoji}{" "}
                    {FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES[rating.feedbackCategory as keyof typeof FEEDBACK_CATEGORIES].label}
                  </Badge>
                  <p className="text-sm mt-2 font-medium">{rating.reason}</p>
                  {rating.notes && (
                    <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1 italic">"{rating.notes}"</p>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        )}

        {/* Media Tabs */}
        <Tabs defaultValue="photos" className="w-full">
          <TabsList className="grid w-full grid-cols-4">
            <TabsTrigger value="photos" data-testid="tab-photos">
              <ImageIcon className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
              Photos ({photos.length})
            </TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="videos" data-testid="tab-videos">
              <Video className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
              Videos ({videos.length})
            </TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="documents" data-testid="tab-documents">
              <FileText className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
              Documents ({documents.length})
            </TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="upload" data-testid="tab-upload">
              <Upload className="h-4 w-4 mr-2" />
              Upload
            </TabsTrigger>
          </TabsList>

          {/* Photos Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="photos" className="mt-4">
            {photos.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="text-center py-8 text-muted-foreground">
                <ImageIcon className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-2 opacity-50" />
                <p>No photos uploaded yet</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                {photos.map((photo) => (
                  <div key={photo.id} className="relative group" data-testid={`photo-${photo.id}`}>
                    <img
                      src={photo.url}
                      alt={photo.caption || 'Property photo'}
                      className="w-full h-48 object-cover rounded-lg"
                    />
                    {photo.caption && (
                      <p className="text-xs mt-1 text-muted-foreground">{photo.caption}</p>
                    )}
                    <Button
                      size="sm"
                      variant="destructive"
                      className="absolute top-2 right-2 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
                      onClick={() => deleteMutation.mutate(photo.id)}
                      data-testid={`button-delete-photo-${photo.id}`}
                    >
                      <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </TabsContent>

          {/* Videos Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="videos" className="mt-4">
            {videos.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="text-center py-8 text-muted-foreground">
                <Video className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-2 opacity-50" />
                <p>No videos uploaded yet</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                {videos.map((video) => (
                  <div key={video.id} className="relative group" data-testid={`video-${video.id}`}>
                    <video
                      src={video.url}
                      controls
                      className="w-full h-48 object-cover rounded-lg bg-black"
                    />
                    {video.caption && (
                      <p className="text-xs mt-1 text-muted-foreground">{video.caption}</p>
                    )}
                    <Button
                      size="sm"
                      variant="destructive"
                      className="absolute top-2 right-2 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
                      onClick={() => deleteMutation.mutate(video.id)}
                      data-testid={`button-delete-video-${video.id}`}
                    >
                      <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </TabsContent>

          {/* Documents Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="documents" className="mt-4">
            {documents.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="text-center py-8 text-muted-foreground">
                <FileText className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-2 opacity-50" />
                <p>No documents uploaded yet</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="space-y-2">
                {documents.map((doc) => (
                  <Card key={doc.id} data-testid={`document-${doc.id}`}>
                    <CardContent className="p-4 flex items-center justify-between">
                      <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
                        <FileText className="h-8 w-8 text-muted-foreground" />
                        <div>
                          <p className="font-medium">{doc.originalName}</p>
                          {doc.documentType && (
                            <Badge variant="outline" className="mt-1">
                              {doc.documentType}
                            </Badge>
                          )}
                          {doc.description && (
                            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">{doc.description}</p>
                          )}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                        <Button
                          size="sm"
                          variant="outline"
                          onClick={() => window.open(doc.url, '_blank')}
                          data-testid={`button-view-doc-${doc.id}`}
                        >
                          <Eye className="h-4 w-4" />
                        </Button>
                        <Button
                          size="sm"
                          variant="destructive"
                          onClick={() => deleteMutation.mutate(doc.id)}
                          data-testid={`button-delete-doc-${doc.id}`}
                        >
                          <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
                        </Button>
                      </div>
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </TabsContent>

          {/* Upload Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="upload" className="mt-4">
            <Card>
              <CardContent className="p-6 space-y-4">
                <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4">
                  {media.length} / 15 files uploaded
                </div>

                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label htmlFor="media-type">Media Type</Label>
                  <Select value={mediaType} onValueChange={(value: any) => setMediaType(value)}>
                    <SelectTrigger id="media-type" data-testid="select-media-type">
                      <SelectValue />
                    </SelectTrigger>
                    <SelectContent>
                      <SelectItem value="photo">Photo</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="video">Video</SelectItem>
                      <SelectItem value="document">Document</SelectItem>
                    </SelectContent>
                  </Select>
                </div>

                {mediaType === 'document' && (
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    <Label htmlFor="document-type">Document Type</Label>
                    <Select value={documentType} onValueChange={setDocumentType}>
                      <SelectTrigger id="document-type" data-testid="select-document-type">
                        <SelectValue />
                      </SelectTrigger>
                      <SelectContent>
                        <SelectItem value="offer">Offer</SelectItem>
                        <SelectItem value="inspection">Inspection Report</SelectItem>
                        <SelectItem value="appraisal">Appraisal</SelectItem>
                        <SelectItem value="floor_plan">Floor Plan</SelectItem>
                        <SelectItem value="listing">Listing Details</SelectItem>
                        <SelectItem value="other">Other</SelectItem>
                      </SelectContent>
                    </Select>
                  </div>
                )}

                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label htmlFor="caption">Caption (Optional)</Label>
                  <Input
                    id="caption"
                    value={caption}
                    onChange={(e) => setCaption(e.target.value)}
                    placeholder="Add a caption..."
                    data-testid="input-caption"
                  />
                </div>

                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label htmlFor="description">Description (Optional)</Label>
                  <Textarea
                    id="description"
                    value={description}
                    onChange={(e) => setDescription(e.target.value)}
                    placeholder="Add a description..."
                    rows={3}
                    data-testid="textarea-description"
                  />
                </div>

                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <Label htmlFor="file-upload">Select Files</Label>
                  <Input
                    id="file-upload"
                    type="file"
                    onChange={handleFileUpload}
                    disabled={uploading || media.length >= 15}
                    multiple
                    accept={
                      mediaType === 'photo' ? 'image/*' :
                      mediaType === 'video' ? 'video/*' :
                      '.pdf,.doc,.docx,.txt'
                    }
                    data-testid="input-file-upload"
                  />
                  {media.length >= 15 && (
                    <p className="text-sm text-destructive">Maximum 15 files reached</p>
                  )}
                </div>

                {uploading && (
                  <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Uploading...</div>
                )}
              </CardContent>
            </Card>
          </TabsContent>
        </Tabs>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}
```

## FILE: client/src/components/TourWizardModal.tsx
```typescript
import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { useMutation, useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { useForm } from "react-hook-form";
import { zodResolver } from "@hookform/resolvers/zod";
import { z } from "zod";
import { useToast } from "@/hooks/use-toast";
import { apiRequest, queryClient } from "@/lib/queryClient";
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { 
  Select,
  SelectContent,
  SelectItem,
  SelectTrigger,
  SelectValue,
} from "@/components/ui/select";
import { 
  Form,
  FormControl,
  FormField,
  FormItem,
  FormLabel,
  FormMessage,
} from "@/components/ui/form";
import { Checkbox } from "@/components/ui/checkbox";
import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area";
import { Progress } from "@/components/ui/progress";
import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";
import { 
  Users, 
  Home, 
  Clock, 
  Route,
  Calendar,
  MapPin,
  Plus,
  X,
  Search,
  ArrowRight,
  ArrowLeft,
  CheckCircle,
  User,
  Building
} from "lucide-react";

interface TourWizardModalProps {
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
}

interface Client {
  id: string;
  firstName: string;
  lastName: string;
  email: string;
  clientType: string;
}

interface Property {
  id: string;
  address: string;
  city: string;
  province: string;
  postalCode: string;
  propertyType: string;
  bedrooms: number;
  bathrooms: number;
  price: number;
  imageUrl?: string;
  description?: string;
  agentId: string;
}

interface ClientGroup {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  createdById: string;
}

interface ManualPropertyData {
  address: string;
  city: string;
  province: string;
  postalCode: string;
  propertyType: string;
  bedrooms: number;
  bathrooms: string;
  price: string;
  description?: string;
}

interface SelectedProperty extends Property {
  scheduledTime?: string;
  estimatedDuration: number;
}

interface TimeBlock {
  startTime: string;
  endTime: string;
  propertyId?: string;
}

interface TourFormData {
  clientId: string;
  groupId?: string;
  scheduledDate: string;
  startTime: string;
  notes?: string;
  properties: SelectedProperty[];
  timeBlocks: TimeBlock[];
}

const manualPropertySchema = z.object({
  address: z.string().min(1, "Address is required"),
  city: z.string().min(1, "City is required"),
  province: z.string().min(1, "Province is required"),
  postalCode: z.string().min(1, "Postal code is required"),
  propertyType: z.enum(["detached", "semi-detached", "townhouse", "condo", "apartment"]),
  bedrooms: z.number().min(0, "Bedrooms must be 0 or more"),
  bathrooms: z.string().min(1, "Bathrooms is required").refine(val => !isNaN(parseFloat(val)) && parseFloat(val) >= 0, "Bathrooms must be a valid positive number"),
  price: z.string().min(1, "Price is required").refine(val => !isNaN(parseFloat(val)) && parseFloat(val) >= 0, "Price must be a valid positive number"),
  description: z.string().optional(),
});

const tourFormSchema = z.object({
  clientId: z.string().min(1, "Client selection is required"),
  groupId: z.string().optional(),
  scheduledDate: z.string().min(1, "Tour date is required"),
  startTime: z.string().min(1, "Start time is required"),
  notes: z.string().optional(),
});

export default function TourWizardModal({ isOpen, onClose }: TourWizardModalProps) {
  const { toast } = useToast();
  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState(1);
  const [selectedClient, setSelectedClient] = useState<Client | null>(null);
  const [selectedGroup, setSelectedGroup] = useState<ClientGroup | null>(null);
  const [selectedProperties, setSelectedProperties] = useState<SelectedProperty[]>([]);
  const [timeBlocks, setTimeBlocks] = useState<TimeBlock[]>([]);
  const [showManualEntry, setShowManualEntry] = useState(false);
  const [mlsSearchQuery, setMlsSearchQuery] = useState("");
  const [optimizedRoute, setOptimizedRoute] = useState<any>(null);

  const steps = [
    { id: 1, title: "Client Selection", description: "Choose client or group" },
    { id: 2, title: "Property Selection", description: "MLS lookup & manual entry" },
    { id: 3, title: "Schedule & Time Blocks", description: "Set times and optimize route" },
    { id: 4, title: "Review & Create", description: "Finalize tour details" },
  ];

  // Fetch clients
  const { data: clients = [], isLoading: clientsLoading } = useQuery<Client[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/clients"],
    enabled: isOpen,
  });

  // Fetch client groups  
  const { data: clientGroups = [], isLoading: groupsLoading } = useQuery<ClientGroup[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/client-groups"],
    enabled: isOpen,
  });

  // Fetch properties (MLS simulation)
  const { data: properties = [], isLoading: propertiesLoading } = useQuery<Property[]>({
    queryKey: ["/api/properties"],
    enabled: isOpen,
  });

  // Form for tour creation
  const form = useForm<TourFormData>({
    resolver: zodResolver(tourFormSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      clientId: "",
      groupId: "",
      scheduledDate: "",
      startTime: "",
      notes: "",
    },
  });

  // Form for manual property entry
  const manualPropertyForm = useForm<ManualPropertyData>({
    resolver: zodResolver(manualPropertySchema),
    defaultValues: {
      address: "",
      city: "",
      province: "",
      postalCode: "",
      propertyType: "detached",
      bedrooms: 0,
      bathrooms: "",
      price: "",
      description: "",
    },
  });

  // Create manual property mutation
  const createPropertyMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (data: ManualPropertyData) => {
      console.log("Creating property with data:", data);
      const response = await apiRequest("POST", "/api/properties", data);
      if (!response.ok) {
        const errorData = await response.json();
        console.error("Property creation failed:", errorData);
        throw new Error(errorData.message || "Failed to create property");
      }
      return response.json();
    },
    onSuccess: (newProperty: Property) => {
      console.log("Property created successfully:", newProperty);
      const selectedProperty: SelectedProperty = {
        ...newProperty,
        estimatedDuration: 30,
      };
      setSelectedProperties(prev => [...prev, selectedProperty]);
      setShowManualEntry(false);
      manualPropertyForm.reset();
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["/api/properties"] });
      toast({
        title: "Property Added",
        description: "Manual property entry has been added to the tour.",
      });
    },
    onError: (error: any) => {
      console.error("Property creation error:", error);
      toast({
        title: "Error",
        description: error.message || "Failed to create property. Please try again.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    },
  });

  // Optimize route mutation
  const optimizeRouteMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (data: { startingAddress: string; properties: SelectedProperty[] }) => {
      const response = await apiRequest("POST", "/api/tours/optimize-route", data);
      return response.json();
    },
    onSuccess: (result) => {
      setOptimizedRoute(result);
      toast({
        title: "Route Optimized",
        description: `Route calculated: ${result.totalDistance}, ${result.totalDuration}`,
      });
    },
    onError: () => {
      toast({
        title: "Optimization Failed",
        description: "Could not optimize route. Please try again.",
        variant: "destructive",
      });
    },
  });

  // Create tour mutation
  const createTourMutation = useMutation({
    mutationFn: async (data: TourFormData) => {
      const tourData = {
        clientId: data.clientId,
        groupId: data.groupId || null,
        scheduledDate: new Date(data.scheduledDate + 'T' + data.startTime),
        startTime: new Date(data.scheduledDate + 'T' + data.startTime),
        notes: data.notes,
        properties: selectedProperties.map((prop, index) => ({
          propertyId: prop.id,
          order: index + 1,
          scheduledTime: prop.scheduledTime ? new Date(data.scheduledDate + 'T' + prop.scheduledTime) : null,
        })),
      };
      
      const response = await apiRequest("POST", "/api/tours", tourData);
      if (!response.ok) {
        const error = await response.json();
        throw { status: response.status, ...error };
      }
      return response.json();
    },
    onSuccess: (tour) => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["/api/tours"] });
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ["/api/stats"] });
      toast({
        title: "Tour Created",
        description: `Tour scheduled successfully for ${selectedClient?.firstName} ${selectedClient?.lastName}`,
      });
      handleClose();
    },
    onError: (error: any) => {
      if (error?.status === 409) {
        toast({
          title: "Duplicate Tour",
          description: "A tour with the same client, date, and properties already exists. Please modify the tour details or select a different date.",
          variant: "destructive",
        });
      } else {
        toast({
          title: "Error",
          description: error?.message || "Failed to create tour. Please try again.",
          variant: "destructive",
        });
      }
    },
  });

  const handleClose = () => {
    setCurrentStep(1);
    setSelectedClient(null);
    setSelectedGroup(null);
    setSelectedProperties([]);
    setTimeBlocks([]);
    setOptimizedRoute(null);
    setShowManualEntry(false);
    form.reset();
    manualPropertyForm.reset();
    onClose();
  };

  const handleNext = () => {
    if (currentStep < 4) {
      setCurrentStep(currentStep + 1);
    }
  };

  const handlePrevious = () => {
    if (currentStep > 1) {
      setCurrentStep(currentStep - 1);
    }
  };

  const handleClientSelect = (client: Client) => {
    setSelectedClient(client);
    form.setValue("clientId", client.id);
  };

  const handleGroupSelect = (group: ClientGroup) => {
    setSelectedGroup(group);
    form.setValue("groupId", group.id);
  };

  const handlePropertySelect = (property: Property) => {
    const isSelected = selectedProperties.find(p => p.id === property.id);
    if (isSelected) {
      setSelectedProperties(prev => prev.filter(p => p.id !== property.id));
    } else {
      const selectedProperty: SelectedProperty = {
        ...property,
        estimatedDuration: 30,
      };
      setSelectedProperties(prev => [...prev, selectedProperty]);
    }
  };

  const handlePropertyTimeUpdate = (propertyId: string, time: string, duration: number) => {
    setSelectedProperties(prev => 
      prev.map(p => 
        p.id === propertyId 
          ? { ...p, scheduledTime: time, estimatedDuration: duration }
          : p
      )
    );
  };

  const handleRemoveProperty = (propertyId: string) => {
    setSelectedProperties(prev => prev.filter(p => p.id !== propertyId));
  };

  const handleOptimizeRoute = () => {
    if (selectedProperties.length > 1) {
      optimizeRouteMutation.mutate({
        startingAddress: "Toronto, ON", // Could be made dynamic
        properties: selectedProperties,
      });
    }
  };

  const handleSubmitManualProperty = (data: ManualPropertyData) => {
    createPropertyMutation.mutate(data);
  };

  const handleCreateTour = (data: TourFormData) => {
    createTourMutation.mutate(data);
  };

  const filteredProperties = properties.filter(property => 
    mlsSearchQuery === "" || 
    property.address.toLowerCase().includes(mlsSearchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
    property.city.toLowerCase().includes(mlsSearchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
    property.propertyType.toLowerCase().includes(mlsSearchQuery.toLowerCase())
  );

  const progressPercentage = (currentStep / 4) * 100;

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  return (
    <Dialog open={isOpen} onOpenChange={handleClose}>
      <DialogContent className="max-w-4xl max-h-[90vh] overflow-hidden">
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle className="text-xl font-semibold">Create New Tour</DialogTitle>
          <div className="space-y-2">
            <Progress value={progressPercentage} className="w-full" />
            <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-muted-foreground">
              {steps.map((step) => (
                <div 
                  key={step.id}
                  className={`flex flex-col items-center ${
                    step.id === currentStep 
                      ? 'text-primary font-medium' 
                      : step.id < currentStep 
                        ? 'text-green-600' 
                        : 'text-muted-foreground'
                  }`}
                >
                  <div className={`w-6 h-6 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-xs mb-1 ${
                    step.id < currentStep 
                      ? 'bg-green-600 text-white' 
                      : step.id === currentStep 
                        ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                        : 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground'
                  }`}>
                    {step.id < currentStep ? <CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3" /> : step.id}
                  </div>
                  <span className="font-medium">{step.title}</span>
                  <span className="text-xs opacity-70">{step.description}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </DialogHeader>

        <ScrollArea className="max-h-[60vh] pr-4">
          <div className="space-y-6">
            {/* Step 1: Client Selection */}
            {currentStep === 1 && (
              <div className="space-y-4" data-testid="tour-wizard-step-1">
                <div className="text-center">
                  <Users className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto text-primary mb-3" />
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Select Client or Group</h3>
                  <p className="text-muted-foreground">Choose who this tour is for</p>
                </div>

                {clientsLoading ? (
                  <div className="text-center">Loading clients...</div>
                ) : (
                  <div className="space-y-4">
                    <div>
                      <Label className="text-sm font-medium mb-3 flex items-center">
                        <User className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                        Individual Clients
                      </Label>
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                        {clients.map((client) => (
                          <Card 
                            key={client.id}
                            className={`cursor-pointer hover:shadow-md transition-all ${
                              selectedClient?.id === client.id 
                                ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5' 
                                : 'hover:border-primary/50'
                            }`}
                            onClick={() => handleClientSelect(client)}
                            data-testid={`client-option-${client.id}`}
                          >
                            <CardContent className="p-3">
                              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                                <div>
                                  <h4 className="font-medium">
                                    {client.firstName} {client.lastName}
                                  </h4>
                                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{client.email}</p>
                                  <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs mt-1">
                                    {client.clientType}
                                  </Badge>
                                </div>
                                {selectedClient?.id === client.id && (
                                  <CheckCircle className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
                                )}
                              </div>
                            </CardContent>
                          </Card>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    <Separator />

                    <div>
                      <Label className="text-sm font-medium mb-3 flex items-center">
                        <Users className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                        Client Groups
                      </Label>
                      {clientGroups.length > 0 ? (
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                          {clientGroups.map((group) => (
                            <Card 
                              key={group.id}
                              className={`cursor-pointer hover:shadow-md transition-all ${
                                selectedGroup?.id === group.id 
                                  ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5' 
                                  : 'hover:border-primary/50'
                              }`}
                              onClick={() => handleGroupSelect(group)}
                              data-testid={`group-option-${group.id}`}
                            >
                              <CardContent className="p-3">
                                <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                                  <div>
                                    <h4 className="font-medium">{group.name}</h4>
                                    <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Group Tour</p>
                                  </div>
                                  {selectedGroup?.id === group.id && (
                                    <CheckCircle className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
                                  )}
                                </div>
                              </CardContent>
                            </Card>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-4">
                          No client groups available
                        </p>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Step 2: Property Selection */}
            {currentStep === 2 && (
              <div className="space-y-4" data-testid="tour-wizard-step-2">
                <div className="text-center">
                  <Building className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto text-primary mb-3" />
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Select Properties</h3>
                  <p className="text-muted-foreground">Choose properties from MLS or add manually</p>
                </div>

                {/* MLS Search & Selection */}
                <Card>
                  <CardHeader>
                    <CardTitle className="text-base flex items-center">
                      <Search className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                      MLS Property Search
                    </CardTitle>
                  </CardHeader>
                  <CardContent className="space-y-4">
                    <div className="flex gap-2">
                      <Input
                        placeholder="Search by address, city, or property type..."
                        value={mlsSearchQuery}
                        onChange={(e) => setMlsSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                        data-testid="mls-search-input"
                      />
                      <Button variant="outline">
                        <Search className="w-4 h-4" />
                      </Button>
                    </div>

                    {propertiesLoading ? (
                      <div className="text-center">Loading properties...</div>
                    ) : (
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-3 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto">
                        {filteredProperties.map((property) => {
                          const isSelected = selectedProperties.find(p => p.id === property.id);
                          return (
                            <Card 
                              key={property.id}
                              className={`cursor-pointer hover:shadow-md transition-all ${
                                isSelected 
                                  ? 'border-primary bg-primary/5' 
                                  : 'hover:border-primary/50'
                              }`}
                              onClick={() => handlePropertySelect(property)}
                              data-testid={`property-option-${property.id}`}
                            >
                              <CardContent className="p-3">
                                <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                                  <div className="flex-1">
                                    <h4 className="font-medium text-sm">{property.address}</h4>
                                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                                      {property.city}, {property.province}
                                    </p>
                                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-1">
                                      <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs">
                                        {property.propertyType}
                                      </Badge>
                                      <span className="text-xs">
                                        {property.bedrooms}br/{property.bathrooms}ba
                                      </span>
                                    </div>
                                    <p className="text-sm font-medium text-green-600 mt-1">
                                      ${property.price.toLocaleString()}
                                    </p>
                                  </div>
                                  {isSelected && (
                                    <CheckCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-primary ml-2" />
                                  )}
                                </div>
                              </CardContent>
                            </Card>
                          );
                        })}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </CardContent>
                </Card>

                {/* Manual Property Entry */}
                <Card>
                  <CardHeader>
                    <CardTitle className="text-base flex items-center justify-between">
                      <span className="flex items-center">
                        <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                        Manual Property Entry
                      </span>
                      <Button
                        variant="outline"
                        size="sm"
                        onClick={() => setShowManualEntry(!showManualEntry)}
                        data-testid="toggle-manual-entry"
                      >
                        {showManualEntry ? "Cancel" : "Add Property"}
                      </Button>
                    </CardTitle>
                  </CardHeader>
                  {showManualEntry && (
                    <CardContent>
                      <Form {...manualPropertyForm}>
                        <form onSubmit={manualPropertyForm.handleSubmit(handleSubmitManualProperty)} className="space-y-4">
                          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                            <FormField
                              control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                              name="address"
                              render={({ field }) => (
                                <FormItem>
                                  <FormLabel>Address</FormLabel>
                                  <FormControl>
                                    <Input {...field} data-testid="input-manual-address" />
                                  </FormControl>
                                  <FormMessage />
                                </FormItem>
                              )}
                            />
                            <FormField
                              control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                              name="city"
                              render={({ field }) => (
                                <FormItem>
                                  <FormLabel>City</FormLabel>
                                  <FormControl>
                                    <Input {...field} data-testid="input-manual-city" />
                                  </FormControl>
                                  <FormMessage />
                                </FormItem>
                              )}
                            />
                          </div>

                          <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                            <FormField
                              control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                              name="province"
                              render={({ field }) => (
                                <FormItem>
                                  <FormLabel>Province</FormLabel>
                                  <FormControl>
                                    <Input {...field} data-testid="input-manual-province" />
                                  </FormControl>
                                  <FormMessage />
                                </FormItem>
                              )}
                            />
                            <FormField
                              control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                              name="postalCode"
                              render={({ field }) => (
                                <FormItem>
                                  <FormLabel>Postal Code</FormLabel>
                                  <FormControl>
                                    <Input {...field} data-testid="input-manual-postal" />
                                  </FormControl>
                                  <FormMessage />
                                </FormItem>
                              )}
                            />
                            <FormField
                              control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                              name="propertyType"
                              render={({ field }) => (
                                <FormItem>
                                  <FormLabel>Property Type</FormLabel>
                                  <Select onValueChange={field.onChange} value={field.value}>
                                    <FormControl>
                                      <SelectTrigger data-testid="select-manual-property-type">
                                        <SelectValue placeholder="Select property type" />
                                      </SelectTrigger>
                                    </FormControl>
                                    <SelectContent>
                                      <SelectItem value="detached">Detached</SelectItem>
                                      <SelectItem value="semi-detached">Semi-Detached</SelectItem>
                                      <SelectItem value="townhouse">Townhouse</SelectItem>
                                      <SelectItem value="condo">Condo</SelectItem>
                                      <SelectItem value="apartment">Apartment</SelectItem>
                                    </SelectContent>
                                  </Select>
                                  <FormMessage />
                                </FormItem>
                              )}
                            />
                          </div>

                          <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                            <FormField
                              control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                              name="bedrooms"
                              render={({ field }) => (
                                <FormItem>
                                  <FormLabel>Bedrooms</FormLabel>
                                  <FormControl>
                                    <Input 
                                      type="number" 
                                      {...field}
                                      onChange={(e) => field.onChange(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}
                                      data-testid="input-manual-bedrooms"
                                    />
                                  </FormControl>
                                  <FormMessage />
                                </FormItem>
                              )}
                            />
                            <FormField
                              control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                              name="bathrooms"
                              render={({ field }) => (
                                <FormItem>
                                  <FormLabel>Bathrooms</FormLabel>
                                  <FormControl>
                                    <Input 
                                      type="number" 
                                      step="0.5"
                                      {...field}
                                      onChange={(e) => field.onChange(e.target.value)}
                                      data-testid="input-manual-bathrooms"
                                    />
                                  </FormControl>
                                  <FormMessage />
                                </FormItem>
                              )}
                            />
                            <FormField
                              control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                              name="price"
                              render={({ field }) => (
                                <FormItem>
                                  <FormLabel>Price ($)</FormLabel>
                                  <FormControl>
                                    <Input 
                                      type="number" 
                                      {...field}
                                      onChange={(e) => field.onChange(e.target.value)}
                                      data-testid="input-manual-price"
                                    />
                                  </FormControl>
                                  <FormMessage />
                                </FormItem>
                              )}
                            />
                          </div>

                          <FormField
                            control={manualPropertyForm.control}
                            name="description"
                            render={({ field }) => (
                              <FormItem>
                                <FormLabel>Description (Optional)</FormLabel>
                                <FormControl>
                                  <Textarea {...field} data-testid="textarea-manual-description" />
                                </FormControl>
                                <FormMessage />
                              </FormItem>
                            )}
                          />

                          <Button 
                            type="submit" 
                            disabled={createPropertyMutation.isPending}
                            data-testid="button-add-manual-property"
                          >
                            {createPropertyMutation.isPending ? "Adding..." : "Add Property"}
                          </Button>
                        </form>
                      </Form>
                    </CardContent>
                  )}
                </Card>

                {/* Selected Properties */}
                {selectedProperties.length > 0 && (
                  <Card>
                    <CardHeader>
                      <CardTitle className="text-base">
                        Selected Properties ({selectedProperties.length})
                      </CardTitle>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent>
                      <div className="space-y-3">
                        {selectedProperties.map((property, index) => (
                          <div 
                            key={property.id} 
                            className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-muted rounded-lg"
                          >
                            <div className="flex-1">
                              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                <span className="text-sm font-medium">#{index + 1}</span>
                                <span className="font-medium">{property.address}</span>
                                <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs">
                                  {property.propertyType}
                                </Badge>
                              </div>
                              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                                {property.city} • {property.bedrooms}br/{property.bathrooms}ba • ${property.price.toLocaleString()}
                              </p>
                            </div>
                            <Button
                              variant="ghost"
                              size="sm"
                              onClick={() => handleRemoveProperty(property.id)}
                              data-testid={`remove-property-${property.id}`}
                            >
                              <X className="w-4 h-4" />
                            </Button>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Step 3: Schedule & Time Blocks */}
            {currentStep === 3 && (
              <div className="space-y-4" data-testid="tour-wizard-step-3">
                <div className="text-center">
                  <Clock className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto text-primary mb-3" />
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Schedule & Optimize Route</h3>
                  <p className="text-muted-foreground">Set tour date, times, and optimize travel route</p>
                </div>

                <Form {...form}>
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                    <FormField
                      control={form.control}
                      name="scheduledDate"
                      render={({ field }) => (
                        <FormItem>
                          <FormLabel>Tour Date</FormLabel>
                          <FormControl>
                            <Input type="date" {...field} data-testid="input-tour-date" />
                          </FormControl>
