                          <FormMessage />
                        </FormItem>
                      )}
                    />
                    <FormField
                      control={form.control}
                      name="startTime"
                      render={({ field }) => (
                        <FormItem>
                          <FormLabel>Start Time</FormLabel>
                          <FormControl>
                            <Input type="time" {...field} data-testid="input-tour-start-time" />
                          </FormControl>
                          <FormMessage />
                        </FormItem>
                      )}
                    />
                  </div>
                </Form>

                {/* Property Time Blocks */}
                {selectedProperties.length > 0 && (
                  <Card>
                    <CardHeader>
                      <CardTitle className="text-base flex items-center justify-between">
                        Property Schedule
                        <Button
                          variant="outline"
                          size="sm"
                          onClick={handleOptimizeRoute}
                          disabled={selectedProperties.length < 2 || optimizeRouteMutation.isPending}
                          data-testid="button-optimize-route"
                        >
                          <Route className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                          {optimizeRouteMutation.isPending ? "Optimizing..." : "Optimize Route"}
                        </Button>
                      </CardTitle>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent className="space-y-4">
                      {selectedProperties.map((property, index) => (
                        <div key={property.id} className="space-y-2">
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <span className="font-medium">#{index + 1}</span>
                            <span className="flex-1">{property.address}</span>
                          </div>
                          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 ml-8">
                            <div>
                              <Label className="text-xs">Scheduled Time</Label>
                              <Input
                                type="time"
                                value={property.scheduledTime || ""}
                                onChange={(e) => handlePropertyTimeUpdate(property.id, e.target.value, property.estimatedDuration)}
                                data-testid={`time-input-${property.id}`}
                              />
                            </div>
                            <div>
                              <Label className="text-xs">Duration (minutes)</Label>
                              <Input
                                type="number"
                                value={property.estimatedDuration}
                                onChange={(e) => handlePropertyTimeUpdate(property.id, property.scheduledTime || "", parseInt(e.target.value) || 30)}
                                data-testid={`duration-input-${property.id}`}
                              />
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      ))}

                      {optimizedRoute && (
                        <div className="mt-4 p-3 bg-green-50 rounded-lg border border-green-200">
                          <h4 className="font-medium text-green-800 mb-2">Optimized Route</h4>
                          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm">
                            <div>
                              <span className="text-green-700">Total Distance:</span>
                              <span className="font-medium ml-2">{optimizedRoute.totalDistance}</span>
                            </div>
                            <div>
                              <span className="text-green-700">Total Duration:</span>
                              <span className="font-medium ml-2">{optimizedRoute.totalDuration}</span>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Step 4: Review & Create */}
            {currentStep === 4 && (
              <div className="space-y-4" data-testid="tour-wizard-step-4">
                <div className="text-center">
                  <CheckCircle className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto text-green-600 mb-3" />
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Review & Create Tour</h3>
                  <p className="text-muted-foreground">Confirm all details before creating the tour</p>
                </div>

                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                  {/* Tour Details */}
                  <Card>
                    <CardHeader>
                      <CardTitle className="text-base">Tour Details</CardTitle>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent className="space-y-3">
                      <div>
                        <Label className="text-sm font-medium">Client</Label>
                        <p className="text-sm">
                          {selectedClient?.firstName} {selectedClient?.lastName} ({selectedClient?.clientType})
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      {selectedGroup && (
                        <div>
                          <Label className="text-sm font-medium">Group</Label>
                          <p className="text-sm">{selectedGroup.name}</p>
                        </div>
                      )}
                      <div>
                        <Label className="text-sm font-medium">Date & Time</Label>
                        <p className="text-sm">
                          {form.watch("scheduledDate")} at {form.watch("startTime")}
                        </p>
                      </div>
                      <div>
                        <Label className="text-sm font-medium">Properties</Label>
                        <p className="text-sm">{selectedProperties.length} properties selected</p>
                      </div>
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>

                  {/* Property List */}
                  <Card>
                    <CardHeader>
                      <CardTitle className="text-base">Property Itinerary</CardTitle>
                    </CardHeader>
                    <CardContent>
                      <div className="space-y-2">
                        {selectedProperties.map((property, index) => (
                          <div key={property.id} className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                            <span className="font-medium">#{index + 1}</span>
                            <div className="flex-1">
                              <p className="font-medium">{property.address}</p>
                              <p className="text-muted-foreground">
                                {property.scheduledTime || "Time TBD"} • {property.estimatedDuration}min
                              </p>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </CardContent>
                  </Card>
                </div>

                {/* Additional Notes */}
                <Form {...form}>
                  <FormField
                    control={form.control}
                    name="notes"
                    render={({ field }) => (
                      <FormItem>
                        <FormLabel>Additional Notes (Optional)</FormLabel>
                        <FormControl>
                          <Textarea 
                            placeholder="Add any special instructions or notes for this tour..."
                            {...field} 
                            data-testid="textarea-tour-notes"
                          />
                        </FormControl>
                        <FormMessage />
                      </FormItem>
                    )}
                  />
                </Form>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </ScrollArea>

        {/* Navigation Buttons */}
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center pt-4 border-t">
          <Button 
            variant="outline" 
            onClick={handlePrevious}
            disabled={currentStep === 1}
            data-testid="button-wizard-previous"
          >
            <ArrowLeft className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
            Previous
          </Button>

          <div className="flex gap-2">
            <Button variant="ghost" onClick={handleClose} data-testid="button-wizard-cancel">
              Cancel
            </Button>
            
            {currentStep < 4 ? (
              <Button 
                onClick={handleNext}
                disabled={
                  (currentStep === 1 && !selectedClient) ||
                  (currentStep === 2 && selectedProperties.length === 0)
                }
                data-testid="button-wizard-next"
              >
                Next
                <ArrowRight className="w-4 w-4 ml-2" />
              </Button>
            ) : (
              <Button 
                onClick={form.handleSubmit(handleCreateTour)}
                disabled={createTourMutation.isPending || !form.watch("scheduledDate") || !form.watch("startTime")}
                data-testid="button-create-tour"
              >
                {createTourMutation.isPending ? "Creating..." : "Create Tour"}
              </Button>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}```

## FILE: client/src/components/AgentSidebar.tsx
```typescript
import { useState } from "react";
import { useLocation } from "wouter";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";
import {
  Sidebar,
  SidebarContent,
  SidebarGroup,
  SidebarGroupContent,
  SidebarGroupLabel,
  SidebarHeader,
  SidebarMenu,
  SidebarMenuButton,
  SidebarMenuItem,
  SidebarRail,
} from "@/components/ui/sidebar";
import {
  LayoutDashboard,
  Users,
  Calendar,
  FileText,
  BarChart3,
  Camera,
  Settings,
  Palette,
  ChevronRight,
  Home,
  Clock,
  MapPin,
  FolderOpen,
  TrendingUp,
  Image,
  Brush
} from "lucide-react";

interface AgentSidebarProps {
  activeSection?: string;
  onSectionChange?: (section: string) => void;
  pendingRequests?: number;
  upcomingTours?: number;
}

export default function AgentSidebar({ 
  activeSection = "dashboard", 
  onSectionChange,
  pendingRequests = 0,
  upcomingTours = 0
}: AgentSidebarProps) {
  const [, setLocation] = useLocation();
  const [expandedGroups, setExpandedGroups] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set(['main']));

  const toggleGroup = (groupKey: string) => {
    const newExpanded = new Set(expandedGroups);
    if (newExpanded.has(groupKey)) {
      newExpanded.delete(groupKey);
    } else {
      newExpanded.add(groupKey);
    }
    setExpandedGroups(newExpanded);
  };

  const handleSectionClick = (section: string) => {
    onSectionChange?.(section);
    
    // Navigate to the appropriate route based on section
    switch (section) {
      case 'clients':
        setLocation('/clients');
        break;
      case 'dashboard':
        setLocation('/');
        break;
      case 'tours':
        setLocation('/tours');
        break;
      case 'documents':
        setLocation('/documents');
        break;
      case 'reports':
        setLocation('/reports');
        break;
      case 'media':
        setLocation('/media');
        break;
      default:
        // For sections without dedicated pages, just update state
        break;
    }
  };

  const menuGroups = [
    {
      key: "main",
      label: "Main Navigation",
      items: [
        {
          key: "dashboard",
          label: "Dashboard",
          icon: LayoutDashboard,
          badge: upcomingTours > 0 ? upcomingTours : undefined,
          testId: "sidebar-dashboard"
        },
        {
          key: "clients",
          label: "Clients",
          icon: Users,
          badge: undefined,
          testId: "sidebar-clients"
        },
        {
          key: "tours",
          label: "Tours & Scheduling",
          icon: Calendar,
          badge: pendingRequests > 0 ? pendingRequests : undefined,
          testId: "sidebar-tours"
        },
        {
          key: "documents",
          label: "Documents",
          icon: FileText,
          badge: undefined,
          testId: "sidebar-documents"
        },
        {
          key: "reports",
          label: "Reports",
          icon: BarChart3,
          badge: undefined,
          testId: "sidebar-reports"
        },
        {
          key: "media",
          label: "Media",
          icon: Camera,
          badge: undefined,
          testId: "sidebar-media"
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      key: "settings",
      label: "Settings & Configuration",
      items: [
        {
          key: "branding",
          label: "Branding & Settings",
          icon: Palette,
          badge: undefined,
          testId: "sidebar-branding"
        }
      ]
    }
  ];

  return (
    <Sidebar className="border-r border-border" data-testid="agent-sidebar">
      <SidebarHeader className="border-b border-border p-4">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Home className="h-5 w-5 text-primary" />
          <span className="font-semibold text-primary">Agent Portal</span>
        </div>
      </SidebarHeader>

      <SidebarContent className="p-2">
        {menuGroups.map((group) => (
          <SidebarGroup key={group.key}>
            <SidebarGroupLabel className="px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">
              <Button
                variant="ghost"
                size="sm"
                className="w-full justify-between p-0 h-auto font-medium"
                onClick={() => toggleGroup(group.key)}
                data-testid={`sidebar-group-${group.key}`}
              >
                {group.label}
                <ChevronRight 
                  className={`h-3 w-3 transition-transform ${
                    expandedGroups.has(group.key) ? 'rotate-90' : ''
                  }`} 
                />
              </Button>
            </SidebarGroupLabel>
            
            {expandedGroups.has(group.key) && (
              <SidebarGroupContent className="mt-2">
                <SidebarMenu>
                  {group.items.map((item) => (
                    <SidebarMenuItem key={item.key}>
                      <SidebarMenuButton
                        asChild
                        isActive={activeSection === item.key}
                        className="w-full justify-start"
                      >
                        <Button
                          variant={activeSection === item.key ? "secondary" : "ghost"}
                          size="sm"
                          className="w-full justify-start gap-3 px-3 py-2"
                          onClick={() => handleSectionClick(item.key)}
                          data-testid={item.testId}
                        >
                          <item.icon className="h-4 w-4" />
                          <span className="flex-1 text-left">{item.label}</span>
                          {item.badge && (
                            <Badge 
                              variant="secondary" 
                              className="ml-auto h-5 px-1.5 text-xs"
                              data-testid={`${item.testId}-badge`}
                            >
                              {item.badge}
                            </Badge>
                          )}
                        </Button>
                      </SidebarMenuButton>
                    </SidebarMenuItem>
                  ))}
                </SidebarMenu>
              </SidebarGroupContent>
            )}
          </SidebarGroup>
        ))}

        <Separator className="my-4" />

        {/* Quick Stats */}
        <SidebarGroup>
          <SidebarGroupLabel className="px-2 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">
            Quick Stats
          </SidebarGroupLabel>
          <SidebarGroupContent className="mt-2 space-y-2">
            <div className="px-3 py-2 rounded-md bg-muted/50">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                <Clock className="h-4 w-4 text-primary" />
                <span className="text-muted-foreground">Today's Tours:</span>
                <span className="font-medium ml-auto" data-testid="sidebar-today-tours">
                  {upcomingTours}
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="px-3 py-2 rounded-md bg-muted/50">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                <MapPin className="h-4 w-4 text-primary" />
                <span className="text-muted-foreground">Pending:</span>
                <span className="font-medium ml-auto" data-testid="sidebar-pending-requests">
                  {pendingRequests}
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </SidebarGroupContent>
        </SidebarGroup>
      </SidebarContent>

      <SidebarRail />
    </Sidebar>
  );
}```

## FILE: vite.config.ts
```typescript
import { defineConfig } from "vite";
import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react";
import path from "path";
import runtimeErrorOverlay from "@replit/vite-plugin-runtime-error-modal";

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [
    react(),
    runtimeErrorOverlay(),
    ...(process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production" &&
    process.env.REPL_ID !== undefined
      ? [
          await import("@replit/vite-plugin-cartographer").then((m) =>
            m.cartographer(),
          ),
          await import("@replit/vite-plugin-dev-banner").then((m) =>
            m.devBanner(),
          ),
        ]
      : []),
  ],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      "@": path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "client", "src"),
      "@shared": path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "shared"),
      "@assets": path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "attached_assets"),
    },
  },
  root: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "client"),
  build: {
    outDir: path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "dist/public"),
    emptyOutDir: true,
  },
  server: {
    fs: {
      strict: true,
      deny: ["**/.*"],
    },
  },
});

✓ Client Files

  - Utility functions and hooks

  - tailwind.config.ts: Styling configuration
